Kb=вҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–вҲһвүӨmaxвҒЎ{вҖ–vвҖ–вҲһ,вҖ–wвҖ–вҲһ}subscriptрқҗҫрқ‘Ҹsubscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Өsubscriptnormрқ‘Јsubscriptnormрқ‘ӨK\_{b}=\|v-w\|\_{\infty}\leq\max\{\|v\|\_{\infty},\|w\|\_{\infty}\}; finally,
n=vвҲ§вӢ…wрқ‘ӣfragmentsfragmentsвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘Өn=v\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}w, nv=вҖ–vвҖ–1вҲ’nsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1рқ‘ӣn\_{v}=\|v\|\_{1}-n, and nw=вҖ–wвҖ–1вҲ’nsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptnormрқ‘Ө1рқ‘ӣn\_{w}=\|w\|\_{1}-n, so nv+nw=вҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө1n\_{v}+n\_{w}=\|v-w\|\_{1}.

{toappendix}

### 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities

In this section, we include a few useful concentration inequalities for functions of random variables that are used throughout our VSA analysis.

Let f:О©1Г—вҖҰГ—О©nвҶ’в„қ:рқ‘“вҶ’subscriptО©1вҖҰsubscriptО©рқ‘ӣв„қf:\Omega\_{1}\times\ldots\times\Omega\_{n}\to\mathbb{R} be an arbitrary function on nрқ‘ӣn variables.

##### Definition 24.

A function f:О©1Г—вҖҰГ—О©nвҶ’в„қ:рқ‘“вҶ’subscriptО©1вҖҰsubscriptО©рқ‘ӣв„қf:\Omega\_{1}\times\ldots\times\Omega\_{n}\to\mathbb{R} has *bounded differences with constants {ci}iвҲҲ[n]subscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ӣ\{c\_{i}\}\_{i\in[n]}* if for all x1вҲҲО©1,вҖҰ,xnвҲҲО©nformulae-sequencesubscriptрқ‘Ҙ1

subscriptО©1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣsubscriptО©рқ‘ӣx\_{1}\in\Omega\_{1},\ldots,x\_{n}\in\Omega\_{n} and all iвҲҲ[n]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ӣi\in[n],

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | supyвҲҲО©i|fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xiвҲ’1,xi,xi+1,вҖҰ,xn)вҲ’fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xiвҲ’1,y,xi+1,вҖҰ,xn)|вүӨcisubscriptsupremumрқ‘ҰsubscriptО©рқ‘–рқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1рқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–\sup\_{y\in\Omega\_{i}}\left|f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{i-1},x\_{i},x\_{i+1},\ldots,x\_{n})-f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{i-1},y,x\_{i+1},\ldots,x\_{n})\right|\leq c\_{i} |  |

When we want to study how fрқ‘“f applied to a random variable Xрқ‘ӢX concentrates around its mean рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)], the most standard tool is McDiarmidвҖҷs inequality.
The usual form of McDiarmidвҖҷs inequality is the following statement:

##### Theorem 25.

Let X=(X1,вҖҰ,Xn)рқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX=(X\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n}) be a tuple of independent random variables supported on О©1,вҖҰ,О©n

subscriptО©1вҖҰsubscriptО©рқ‘ӣ\Omega\_{1},\ldots,\Omega\_{n}, respectively.
If fрқ‘“f has bounded differences with constants c1,вҖҰ,cn

subscriptрқ‘җ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘ӣc\_{1},\ldots,c\_{n}, then:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]>t]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ў\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]>t\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2вҲ‘i=1nci2)absent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ӣsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{\sum\_{i=1}^{n}c\_{i}^{2}}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]<вҲ’t]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ў\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]<-t\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2вҲ‘i=1nci2)absent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ӣsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{\sum\_{i=1}^{n}c\_{i}^{2}}\right) |  |

We now derive a standard variant (CorollaryВ [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) of McDiarmid that applies when the bounded differences hold with high probability.
This is not a novel modification, but we include it for completeness.
The corollary follows from the following lemma, which we will also use throughout our VSA analysis.

##### Lemma 26.

Let Xрқ‘ӢX be a random variable taking values in domain Dрқҗ·D, e.g. D=в„қnрқҗ·superscriptв„қрқ‘ӣD={\mathbb{R}}^{n}.
Let fрқ‘“f and gрқ‘”g map from Dрқҗ·D to в„қв„қ{\mathbb{R}}, such that PrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вү fвҖӢ(X)]вүӨОҙPrрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝ\Pr[g(X)\neq f(X)]\leq\delta, with gвҖӢ(X)=0рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣ0g(X)=0 when gвҖӢ(X)вү fвҖӢ(X)рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣg(X)\neq f(X), and supxвҲҲDfвҖӢ(x)вүӨMsubscriptsupremumрқ‘Ҙрқҗ·рқ‘“рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Җ\sup\_{x\in D}f(x)\leq M for a value MвҲҲв„қрқ‘Җв„қM\in{\mathbb{R}}.
Then

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]>t+ОҙвҖӢM]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ўрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\displaystyle\Pr[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]>t+\delta M] | вүӨPrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]>t]+ОҙabsentPrрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ўрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr[g(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]>t]+\delta |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]<вҲ’tвҲ’ОҙвҖӢM]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ўрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\displaystyle\Pr[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]<-t-\delta M] | вүӨPrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]<вҲ’t]+ОҙabsentPrрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ўрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr[g(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]<-t]+\delta |  |

##### Proof.

Let BрқҗөB be the вҖңbad subsetвҖқ of Dрқҗ·D where gвҖӢ(X)вү fвҖӢ(X)рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣg(X)\neq f(X).
Here рқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)] is close but not equal to рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ\displaystyle{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)] | =вҲ‘xвҲүBPrвҒЎ[X=x]вӢ…fвҖӢ(x)+вҲ‘xвҲҲBPrвҒЎ[X=x]вӢ…fвҖӢ(x)absentsubscriptрқ‘ҘрқҗөвӢ…Prрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ҙрқ‘“рқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘ҘрқҗөвӢ…Prрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ҙрқ‘“рқ‘Ҙ\displaystyle=\sum\_{x\notin B}\Pr[X=x]\cdot f(x)+\sum\_{x\in B}\Pr[X=x]\cdot f(x) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨвҲ‘(x)вҲүBPrвҒЎ[X=x]вӢ…gвҖӢ(x)+ОҙвҖӢM=рқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]+ОҙвҖӢMabsentsubscriptрқ‘ҘрқҗөвӢ…Prрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ҙрқ‘”рқ‘Ҙрқӣҝрқ‘Җрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\displaystyle\leq\sum\_{(x)\notin B}\Pr[X=x]\cdot g(x)+\delta M={\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]+\delta M |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Similarly,В вҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]Similarly,В рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ\displaystyle\text{Similarly, }{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)] | вүҘрқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]вҲ’ОҙвҖӢMabsentрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\displaystyle\geq{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]-\delta M |  |

Using this relationship between the means of fвҖӢ(X)рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣf(X) and gвҖӢ(X)рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣg(X), we have.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүҘtвҖІ]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІ\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\geq t^{\prime}\right] | вүӨPrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүҘtвҖІ|fвҖӢ(X)=gвҖӢ(X)]вӢ…PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)=gвҖӢ(X)]+ОҙabsentвӢ…Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣconditionalsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘”рқ‘ӢPrрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\geq t^{\prime}\,|\,f(X)=g(X)\right]\cdot\Pr[f(X)=g(X)]+\delta |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨPrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүҘtвҖІ|fвҖӢ(X)=gвҖӢ(X)]вӢ…PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)=gвҖӢ(X)]+ОҙabsentвӢ…Prрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣconditionalsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘”рқ‘ӢPrрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr\left[g(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\geq t^{\prime}\,|\,f(X)=g(X)\right]\cdot\Pr[f(X)=g(X)]+\delta |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨPrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүҘtвҖІ]+ОҙabsentPrрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr[g(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\geq t^{\prime}]+\delta |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨPrвҒЎ[gвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]вүҘtвҖІвҲ’ОҙвҖӢM]+ОҙabsentPrрқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІрқӣҝрқ‘Җрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\Pr[g(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]\geq t^{\prime}-\delta M]+\delta |  |

The final line comes from the fact that рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүҘрқ”јвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(X)]вҲ’ОҙвҖӢMрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘”рқ‘Ӣрқӣҝрқ‘Җ{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\geq{\mathbb{E}}[g(X)]-\delta M.
Letting tвҖІ=t+ОҙвҖӢMsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІрқ‘Ўрқӣҝрқ‘Җt^{\prime}=t+\delta M yields the desired bound.
The upper bound for PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]вүӨвҲ’tвҖІ]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣsuperscriptрқ‘ЎвҖІ\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]\leq-t^{\prime}\right] is analogous.
вҲҺ

##### Corollary 27.

Let X1,вҖҰ,Xn

subscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n} be independent random variables supported on О©1,вҖҰ,О©n

subscriptО©1вҖҰsubscriptО©рқ‘ӣ\Omega\_{1},\ldots,\Omega\_{n}, respectively.
Define M:=supx1,вҖҰ,xn|fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xn)|assignрқ‘Җsubscriptsupremum

subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣM:=\sup\_{x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{n}}|f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{n})|.
If with probability 1вҲ’Оҙ1рқӣҝ1-\delta over X1,вҖҰ,Xn

subscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n}, the function fрқ‘“f has bounded differences with constants c1,вҖҰ,cn

subscriptрқ‘җ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘ӣc\_{1},\ldots,c\_{n}, i.e. there is a set SвҠҶО©рқ‘ҶО©S\subseteq\Omega with PrвҒЎ[XвҲҲS]=1вҲ’ОҙPrрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ҷ1рқӣҝ\Pr[X\in S]=1-\delta such that for all (x1,вҖҰ,xn)вҲҲSsubscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ҷ(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{n})\in S and iвҲҲ[n]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ӣi\in[n], we satisfy

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | supyвҲҲО©i|fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xiвҲ’1,xi,xi+1,вҖҰ,xn)вҲ’fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xiвҲ’1,y,xi+1,вҖҰ,xn)|вүӨcisubscriptsupremumрқ‘ҰsubscriptО©рқ‘–рқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1рқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–\sup\_{y\in\Omega\_{i}}\left|f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{i-1},x\_{i},x\_{i+1},\ldots,x\_{n})-f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{i-1},y,x\_{i+1},\ldots,x\_{n})\right|\leq c\_{i} |  |

then both of the following inequalities hold.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]>t+ОҙвҖӢM]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ўрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]>t+\delta M\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2вҲ‘i=1nci2)+Оҙabsent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ӣsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2рқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{\sum\_{i=1}^{n}c\_{i}^{2}}\right)+\delta |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Pr[f(X)вҲ’рқ”ј[f(X)]<вҲ’tвҲ’ОҙM]]\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]<-t-\delta M]\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2вҲ‘i=1nci2)+Оҙabsent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ӣsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2рқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{\sum\_{i=1}^{n}c\_{i}^{2}}\right)+\delta |  |

##### Proof.

Apply LemmaВ [26](#Thmtheorem26 "Lemma 26. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") to fрқ‘“f and the function gрқ‘”g defined as taking the same value of fрқ‘“f for X1,вҖҰ,Xn

subscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n} such that the bounded differences hold, and zero otherwise. Then, we apply TheoremВ [25](#Thmtheorem25 "Theorem 25. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") toВ gрқ‘”g.
вҲҺ

There is also a version of McDiarmidвҖҷs inequality that incorporates variances; we refer to it as the вҖңBernstein form of McDiarmidвҖҷs Inequality:вҖқ

##### Theorem 28 ([ying\_mcdiarmids\_2004]).

Let X=(X1,вҖҰ,Xn)рқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX=(X\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n}) be a tuple of independent random variables supported on О©вүЎвҲҸiвҲҲ[n]О©iО©subscriptproductрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ӣsubscriptО©рқ‘–\Omega\equiv\prod\_{i\in[n]}\Omega\_{i}.
For function f:О©вҶ’IвҖӢR:рқ‘“вҶ’О©IRf:\Omega\rightarrow\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}} and xвҲҲО©,iвҲҲ[n],yвҲҲО©iformulae-sequenceрқ‘ҘО©formulae-sequenceрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ӣрқ‘ҰsubscriptО©рқ‘–x\in\Omega,i\in[n],y\in\Omega\_{i}, let
giвҖӢ(x,y)вүЎfвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,xiвҲ’1,y,xi+1,вҖҰ,xn)subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1рқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ӣg\_{i}(x,y)\equiv f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{i-1},y,x\_{i+1},\ldots,x\_{n}).
(Note that giвҖӢ(x,y)subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұg\_{i}(x,y) does not depend on xisubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x\_{i}.)
Let

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | VariвҖӢ(f)subscriptVarрқ‘–рқ‘“\displaystyle{\textbf{Var}}\_{i}(f) | вүЎsupxвҲҲО©рқ”јXiвҖӢ[(giвҖӢ(x,Xi)вҲ’рқ”јXiвҖІвҖӢgiвҖӢ(x,XiвҖІ))2]absentsubscriptsupremumрқ‘ҘО©subscriptрқ”јsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘–delimited-[]superscriptsubscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–рқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘–subscriptрқ”јsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–рқ‘Ҙsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІрқ‘–2\displaystyle\equiv\sup\_{x\in\Omega}{\mathbb{E}}\_{X\_{i}}\left[\left(g\_{i}(x,X\_{i})-{\mathbb{E}}\_{X^{\prime}\_{i}}g\_{i}(x,X^{\prime}\_{i})\right)^{2}\right] |  |

Then

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]>t]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ў\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]>t\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2Пғ~вҖӢ(f)+tвҖӢBвҖӢ(f)/3)absent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2~рқңҺрқ‘“рқ‘Ўрқҗөрқ‘“3\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{{\tilde{\sigma}}(f)+tB(f)/3}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[fвҖӢ(X)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]<вҲ’t]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ў\displaystyle\Pr\left[f(X)-{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]<-t\right] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢt2Пғ~вҖӢ(f)+tвҖӢBвҖӢ(f)/3)absent2superscriptрқ‘Ў2~рқңҺрқ‘“рқ‘Ўрқҗөрқ‘“3\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2t^{2}}{{\tilde{\sigma}}(f)+tB(f)/3}\right) |  |

We will also need this known concentration bound for Rademacher random variables.

##### Theorem 29.

Let X1,вҖҰ,Xn

subscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣX\_{1},\ldots,X\_{n} be independent Rademacher random variables. Let (a1,вҖҰ,an)subscriptрқ‘Һ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Һрқ‘ӣ(a\_{1},\ldots,a\_{n}) be an arbitrary vector in в„қnsuperscriptв„қрқ‘ӣ{\mathbb{R}}^{n}. Then,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[вҲ‘i=1naiвҖӢXiвүҘtвҖӢвҖ–aвҖ–2]вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’t22)Prsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘Һрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘–рқ‘Ўsubscriptnormрқ‘Һ2superscriptрқ‘Ў22\Pr\left[\sum\_{i=1}^{n}a\_{i}X\_{i}\geq t\|a\|\_{2}\right]\leq\exp\left(-\frac{t^{2}}{2}\right) |  |

### 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss

In В§[4.1](#S4.SS1 "4.1 Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we analyze MAP-I bundling, including the relation of norm estimation to distance, set intersection, and angle estimation, and discuss how the JL perspective extends to the sparse JL and Subsampled Randomized Hadamard Transforms (SRHTs).

Next, in В§[4.2](#S4.SS2 "4.2 Rotations for Encoding Sequences вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we analyze the VSA dimension needed to reliably estimate the intersection of two *sequences* of sets, as encoded using rotations, in both a general and a more restricted setting.
This entails proving the JL property for a specific kind of random matrix with dependent entries.

Finally, in В§[4.3](#S4.SS3 "4.3 Binding вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we analyze intersection of bundles of bound pairs and bundles of kрқ‘ҳk-wise bindings.
Again, we establish the JL property for a random matrix with dependent entries.
While bundles of key-value bindings have been analyzed before, bundles of kрқ‘ҳk-wise bindings have not.

#### 4.1 Bundling and Set Intersection

The results in this section may apply to VSAs beyond just MAP-I where the bundling operator is addition over the real numbers.
SectionВ 3.1 of [thomas2021theoretical] gives some representational bounds in that setting.
Though we provide similar bounds, we frame our results using the Johnson-Lindenstrauss (JL) random projection lemma, which provides a simpler yet powerful lens through which to view the MAP-I VSA.
(A connection to JL was briefly mentioned by [kent2020multiplicative], but it did not factor into any capacity analysis there.)

We first introduce the Johnson-Lindenstrauss (JL) lemma:

##### Lemma (Restatement of Lemma [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Suppose SВҜвҲҲ1mвҖӢ{вҲ’1,1}mГ—dВҜрқ‘Ҷ1рқ‘ҡsuperscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘‘{\bar{S}}\in\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\{-1,1\}^{m\times d} is a scaled sign matrix (described in Def.В [2](#Thmtheorem2 "Definition 2. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
Then for given Оҙ,Пө>0

рқӣҝitalic-Пө
0\delta,\epsilon>0 there is m=OвҖӢ(ПөвҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsuperscriptitalic-Пө21рқӣҝm=O(\epsilon^{-2}\log(1/\delta)) such that for given vector vвҲҲIвҖӢRdрқ‘ЈsuperscriptIRрқ‘‘v\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{d}, it holds that вҖ–SВҜвҖӢvвҖ–=вҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢ(1ВұПө)normВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Јplus-or-minus1italic-Пө\|{\bar{S}}v\|=\|v\|(1\pm\epsilon), with failure probability at most Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.

##### Remark 30.

We have a similar result for any matrix Pрқ‘ғP with i.i.d. subGaussian entries.

This approximation bound can be easily translated to a bound for multiple differences of vectors.
The proof is simply the application of of LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") to the OвҖӢ(n2)рқ‘Ӯsuperscriptрқ‘ӣ2O(n^{2}) pairs of differences of vectors of рқ’ұрқ’ұ\mathcal{V}, and a union bound (yielding the logвҒЎnрқ‘ӣ\log n part of the bound).

##### Corollary (Restatement of Corollary [4](#Thmtheorem4 "Corollary 4. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

If random matrix Pрқ‘ғP satisfies the JL property (LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")),
then for given Оҙ,Пө>0

рқӣҝitalic-Пө
0\delta,\epsilon>0, and a set рқ’ұвҠӮIвҖӢRdрқ’ұsuperscriptIRрқ‘‘\mathcal{V}\subset\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{d} of cardinality nрқ‘ӣn,
there is m=OвҖӢ(ПөвҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(n/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsuperscriptitalic-Пө2рқ‘ӣрқӣҝm=O(\epsilon^{-2}\log(n/\delta)) such that
with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, for all pairs v,wвҲҲрқ’ұ

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
рқ’ұv,w\in\mathcal{V},
вҖ–PвҖӢ(vвҲ’w)вҖ–2вҲҲвҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–2вҖӢ(1ВұПө)superscriptnormрқ‘ғрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө2superscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө2plus-or-minus1italic-Пө\|P(v-w)\|^{2}\in\|v-w\|^{2}(1\pm\epsilon).

In other words, the linear mapping Pрқ‘ғP preserves Euclidean distances up to a multiplicative factor of (1ВұПө)plus-or-minus1italic-Пө(1\pm\epsilon).
If vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw are characteristic vectors for sets Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY, then вҖ–vвҲ’yвҖ–2=|XвҖӢО”вҖӢY|superscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ұ2рқ‘ӢО”рқ‘Ң\|v-y\|^{2}=|X\Delta Y|, the cardinality of the symmetric difference of Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY.
Thus, by taking the difference between their VSA representations PвҖӢvрқ‘ғрқ‘ЈPv and PвҖӢvрқ‘ғрқ‘ЈPv, we can estimate how much the sets Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY disagree, with small *relative* error Пөitalic-Пө\epsilon in that estimate, mild dependence on the number of sets we can represent in this way, and no dependence, in the error, on the groundset size nрқ‘ӣn.

However, this doesnвҖҷt say what the needed dimensionality mрқ‘ҡm is, for accurate estimation of the size of the intersection.
We consider this next, using the following standard corollary of LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

##### Corollary (Restatement of Corollary [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Suppose the random matrix Pрқ‘ғP satisfies the JL property (LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
Then for v,wвҲҲIвҖӢRd

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscriptIRрқ‘‘v,w\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{d}, there is m=OвҖӢ(ПөвҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsuperscriptitalic-Пө21рқӣҝm=O(\epsilon^{-2}\log(1/\delta)) so that
vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢw=vвҠӨвҖӢwВұПөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–superscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өitalic-Пөnormрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Өv^{\top}P^{\top}Pw=v^{\top}w\pm\epsilon\|v\|\|w\|
with failure probabilityВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.

##### Proof.

First, suppose vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw are unit vectors.
By LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") and a union bound, with failure probability at most 3вҖӢОҙ3рқӣҝ3\delta we have
vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢv=vвҠӨвҖӢvВұПөsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Јplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Јitalic-Пөv^{\top}P^{\top}Pv=v^{\top}v\pm\epsilon,
wвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢw=wвҠӨвҖӢwВұПөsuperscriptрқ‘Өtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Өtopрқ‘Өitalic-Пөw^{\top}P^{\top}Pw=w^{\top}w\pm\epsilon, and
(v+w)вҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢ(v+w)=(v+w)вҠӨвҖӢ(v+w)Вұ2вҖӢПөsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘Өtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Јрқ‘Өplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘Өtopрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө2italic-Пө(v+w)^{\top}P^{\top}P(v+w)=(v+w)^{\top}(v+w)\pm 2\epsilon.
Since 2вҖӢvвҠӨвҖӢw=(v+w)вҠӨвҖӢ(v+w)вҲ’vвҠӨвҖӢvвҲ’wвҠӨвҖӢw2superscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘Өtopрқ‘Јрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Јsuperscriptрқ‘Өtopрқ‘Ө2v^{\top}w=(v+w)^{\top}(v+w)-v^{\top}v-w^{\top}w and matrix multiplication is an application of a linear operator, an analogous expression holds for vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢwsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өv^{\top}P^{\top}Pw.
Then,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | 2вҖӢ(vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢwвҲ’vвҠӨвҖӢw)=ВұПөВұПөВұ2вҖӢПө=Вұ4вҖӢПө,2superscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өplus-or-minusplus-or-minusitalic-Пөitalic-Пө2italic-Пөplus-or-minus4italic-Пө2(v^{\top}P^{\top}Pw-v^{\top}w)=\pm\epsilon\pm\epsilon\pm 2\epsilon=\pm 4\epsilon, |  |

with failure probability 3вҖӢОҙ3рқӣҝ3\delta.
If vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw are not unit vectors,
we apply this reasoning to v/вҖ–vвҖ–рқ‘Јnormрқ‘Јv/\|v\| and w/вҖ–wвҖ–рқ‘Өnormрқ‘Өw/\|w\|, and then multiply through by вҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–normрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Ө\|v\|\|w\|, getting vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢw=vвҠӨвҖӢwВұ2вҖӢПөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–superscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Ө2italic-Пөnormрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Өv^{\top}P^{\top}Pw=v^{\top}w\pm 2\epsilon\|v\|\|w\|.
That is, the conclusion holds with relative error parameter 2вҖӢПө2italic-Пө2\epsilon and failure probability 3вҖӢОҙ3рқӣҝ3\delta.
We can fold the factors 2 and 3 into the bound for mрқ‘ҡm, and the result follows.
вҲҺ

Beyond the approximation condition, the proof only depends on Pрқ‘ғP being a linear operator.
Suppose Pрқ‘ғP is a scaled sign matrix SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}}, and let v,wвҲҲ{0,1}d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscript01рқ‘‘v,w\in\{0,1\}^{d} be characteristic vectors.
We want vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢw=vвҠӨвҖӢwВұПө0superscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өplus-or-minussuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өsubscriptitalic-Пө0v^{\top}P^{\top}Pw=v^{\top}w\pm\epsilon\_{0}, where Пө0<1/2subscriptitalic-Пө012\epsilon\_{0}<1/2.
Since vвҠӨвҖӢwsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өv^{\top}w is an integer, this assures that vвҠӨвҖӢPвҠӨвҖӢPвҖӢwsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopsuperscriptрқ‘ғtopрқ‘ғрқ‘Өv^{\top}P^{\top}Pw rounds to vвҠӨвҖӢwsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өv^{\top}w.
The next lemma gives conditions on Пөitalic-Пө\epsilon and Оҙрқӣҝ\delta to attain this.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [6](#Thmtheorem6 "Theorem 6. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Suppose random matrix Pрқ‘ғP satisfies the JL property (LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
Given Mрқ‘ҖM pairs of characteristic vectors v,wвҲҲ{0,1}d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscript01рқ‘‘v,w\in\{0,1\}^{d} such that for every pair v,w

рқ‘Јрқ‘Өv,w, вҖ–vвҖ–1вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–1вүӨNsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1subscriptnormрқ‘Ө1рқ‘Ғ\|v\|\_{1}\|w\|\_{1}\leq N, then there is m=OвҖӢ(NвҖӢlogвҒЎ(M/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘Ғрқ‘Җрқӣҝm=O(N\log(M/\delta)) such that вҢҠvвҠӨPвҠӨPwвҢү=vвҠӨw\lfloor v^{\top}P^{\top}Pw\rceil=v^{\top}w for all Mрқ‘ҖM pairs with probability вүҘ1вҲ’Оҙabsent1рқӣҝ\geq 1-\delta.

##### Remark 31.

In particular, this holds for the following special cases.

* вҖў

  Set membership: vрқ‘Јv is a characteristic vector, and wрқ‘Өw is a standard basis vector eisubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘–e\_{i} for iвҲҲ[d]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘‘i\in[d].
  Then, N=вҖ–vвҖ–1рқ‘Ғsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1N=\|v\|\_{1}, M=dрқ‘Җрқ‘‘M=d, and VSA dimension m=O(вҲҘvвҲҘ1log(d/Оҙ)m=O(\|v\|\_{1}\log(d/\delta) suffices.
* вҖў

  To get all pairwise intersections among MOвҖӢ(1)superscriptрқ‘Җрқ‘Ӯ1M^{O(1)} vectors vрқ‘Јv with вҖ–vвҖ–1вүӨNsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1рқ‘Ғ\|v\|\_{1}\leq\sqrt{N}, we can use m=OвҖӢ(NвҖӢlogвҒЎ(M/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘Ғрқ‘Җрқӣҝm=O(N\log(M/\delta)).

##### Proof.

For a given pair of vectors vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw, by CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") it is enough to choose Пө0<1/2subscriptitalic-Пө012\epsilon\_{0}<1/2 and Пө=Пө0/(вҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–)вүҘПө0/Nitalic-Пөsubscriptitalic-Пө0normрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Өsubscriptitalic-Пө0рқ‘Ғ\epsilon=\epsilon\_{0}/(\|v\|\|w\|)\geq\epsilon\_{0}/\sqrt{N}, to achieve the desired accuracy.

If ОҙвҖІsuperscriptрқӣҝвҖІ\delta^{\prime} is the failure probability of CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), then the overall failure probability is at most MвҖӢОҙвҖІрқ‘ҖsuperscriptрқӣҝвҖІM\delta^{\prime}, by a union bound.
Thus for ОҙвҖІ=Оҙ/MsuperscriptрқӣҝвҖІрқӣҝрқ‘Җ\delta^{\prime}=\delta/M and Пөitalic-Пө\epsilon from the JL property equal to Пө0/Nsubscriptitalic-Пө0рқ‘Ғ\epsilon\_{0}/\sqrt{N}, the dimension mрқ‘ҡm of CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") is m=OвҖӢ(NвҖӢlogвҒЎ(M/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘Ғрқ‘Җрқӣҝm=O(N\log(M/\delta)), and
every dot product estimate is accurate to within additiveВ Пө0subscriptitalic-Пө0\epsilon\_{0} with failure probability at mostВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.
The result follows.
вҲҺ

##### Angle estimation

Let Оҳv,wsubscriptОҳ

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө\Theta\_{v,w} denote the angle between vectors vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw.

##### Lemma 32.

Under the conditions of LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), for v,wвҲҲIвҖӢRd

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscriptIRрқ‘‘v,w\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{d}, there is m=OвҖӢ(ПөвҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsuperscriptitalic-Пө21рқӣҝm=O(\epsilon^{-2}\log(1/\delta)) so that cosвҒЎОҳSВҜвҖӢv,SВҜвҖӢw=cosвҒЎОҳv,wВұПөsubscriptОҳ

ВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘ЈВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Өplus-or-minussubscriptОҳ

рқ‘Јрқ‘Өitalic-Пө\cos\Theta\_{{\bar{S}}v,{\bar{S}}w}=\cos\Theta\_{v,w}\pm\epsilon with failure probabilityВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.

##### Proof.

This follows from cosвҒЎОҳv,w=vвҠӨвҖӢwвҖ–vвҖ–вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–subscriptОҳ

рқ‘Јрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өnormрқ‘Јnormрқ‘Ө\cos\Theta\_{v,w}=\frac{v^{\top}w}{\|v\|\|w\|}, and similarly for ОҳSВҜвҖӢv,SВҜвҖӢwsubscriptОҳ

ВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘ЈВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ө\Theta\_{{\bar{S}}v,{\bar{S}}w}; applying CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") to the estimation of vвҠӨвҖӢwsuperscriptрқ‘Јtopрқ‘Өv^{\top}w, вҖ–vвҖ–normрқ‘Ј\|v\|, and вҖ–wвҖ–normрқ‘Ө\|w\|, and finally folding constant-factor increases inВ Пөitalic-Пө\epsilon and Оҙрқӣҝ\delta intoВ mрқ‘ҡm.
вҲҺ

##### 4.1.1 Variations Using Alternative Sketching Matrices

##### Using sparse JL

The sparse JL transform has ПөвҖӢmitalic-Пөрқ‘ҡ\epsilon m nonzero entries per column of Pрқ‘ғP, each entry an independent sign (that is, Вұ1plus-or-minus1\pm 1). Such a matrix, multiplied by a scaling factor, also satisfies LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), as shown in [kane2014sparser, cohen2018simple], and therefore could be used in VSAs with the same performance, at least as far as bundling goes.
However, element-wise product does not seem to be enough to do binding effectively for such a representation, as the element-wise product of sparse vectors is likely to be all zeros.

##### Using Subsampled Randomized Hadamard Transform (SRHT)

The SRHT, described in [boutsidis2013improved], is multiplication by a matrix ZвҖӢHвҖӢDрқ‘Қрқҗ»рқҗ·ZHD, where Dрқҗ·D is a random sign diagonal matrix (random sign flips on the diagonal), Hрқҗ»H is a Hadamard matrix (an orthogonal sign matrix), and Zрқ‘ҚZ simply selects a uniform random subset of the rows (a diagonal binary matrix).
This operation, along with a scaling factor, is shown by [krahmer2011new] to satisfy the conditions of LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), up to needing the larger target dimension m=OвҖӢ(ПөвҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ)вҖӢlog4вҒЎd)рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsuperscriptitalic-Пө21рқӣҝsuperscript4рқ‘‘m=O(\epsilon^{-2}\log(1/\delta)\log^{4}d), that is, with an additional factor of log4вҒЎdsuperscript4рқ‘‘\log^{4}d.
While for many applications, a useful property of SRHT is that ZвҖӢHвҖӢDвҖӢvрқ‘Қрқҗ»рқҗ·рқ‘ЈZHDv is rapidly computed, here the main attraction is that the generation or storage of random sign values is greatly reduced; entries of the Hрқҗ»H matrix are readily computed using bitwise operations on the entry indices.

#### 4.2 Rotations for Encoding Sequences

For scaled sign matrices, using a rotation (i.e. a permutation that is a single large cycle), we can store length-LрқҗҝL sequences of vectors with an error bound that grows quadratically with LрқҗҝL.
It is possible that there is a better general bound than this; we found better performance in a special case.
If the vectors are, in particular, characteristic vectors, so that a sequence of symbols is being stored (and not e.g. a sequence of embeddings), then better error behavior (that depends on how much the vectors overlap, rather than naively on LрқҗҝL) typically occurs.

Before further definition and analysis, we have some lemmas useful for the analysis.

##### Lemma 33.

Say we sample independent scaled random sign matrices P1,P2вҲҲ{Вұ1}mГ—d

subscriptрқ‘ғ1subscriptрқ‘ғ2

##### Lemma 34.

x2вҠӨвҖӢSВҜ2вҠӨвҖӢ(RrвҖӢSВҜ)2вҖӢy2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҙ2topsuperscriptsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ2topsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘…рқ‘ҹВҜрқ‘Ҷ2subscriptрқ‘Ұ2x\_{2}^{\top}{\bar{S}}\_{2}^{\top}(R^{r}{\bar{S}})\_{2}y\_{2}. Adding these bounds, and taking a union bound on the failure probability, yields the result for unit vectors. The claim about non-unit vectors follows immediately.

##### Definition 35.

##### Proof.

Assuming the approximation bounds of LemmaВ [34](#Thmtheorem34 "Lemma 34. вҖЈ 4.2 Rotations for Encoding Sequences вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") hold for several instances, we have that

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | вҖ–SВҜR,LвҖӢvвҖ–2superscriptnormsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ  рқ‘…рқҗҝрқ‘Ј2\displaystyle\|{\bar{S}}\_{R,L}v\|^{2} | =вҖ–вҲ‘0вүӨj<LRjвҖӢSВҜвҖӢv(j)вҖ–2absentsuperscriptnormsubscript0рқ‘—рқҗҝsuperscriptрқ‘…рқ‘—ВҜрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—2\displaystyle=\|\sum\_{0\leq j<L}R^{j}{\bar{S}}v\_{(j)}\|^{2} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =вҲ‘0вүӨj,jвҖІ<Lv(jвҖІ)вҠӨвҖӢSВҜвҠӨвҖӢ(RвҠӨ)jвҖІвҖӢRjвҖӢSВҜвҖӢv(j)absentsubscriptformulae-sequence0рқ‘—superscriptрқ‘—вҖІрқҗҝsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘Јsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІtopsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtopsuperscriptsuperscriptрқ‘…topsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІsuperscriptрқ‘…рқ‘—ВҜрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—\displaystyle=\sum\_{0\leq j,j^{\prime}<L}v\_{(j^{\prime})}^{\top}{\bar{S}}^{\top}(R^{\top})^{j^{\prime}}R^{j}{\bar{S}}v\_{(j)} |  |
|  |  |  |  |

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨвҖ–vвҖ–2вҖӢ(1ВұПө)+2вҖӢвҲ‘0вүӨjвҖІ<j<LПөвҖӢвҖ–v(jвҖІ)вҖ–вҲ—вҖ–v(j)вҖ–absentsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј2plus-or-minus1italic-Пө2subscript0superscriptрқ‘—вҖІрқ‘—рқҗҝitalic-Пөnormsubscriptрқ‘Јsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІnormsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—\displaystyle\leq\|v\|^{2}(1\pm\epsilon)+2\sum\_{0\leq j^{\prime}<j<L}\epsilon\|v\_{(j^{\prime})}\|\*\|v\_{(j)}\| |  |

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

as claimed.
Here we use that for vector zвҲҲIвҖӢRLрқ‘§superscriptIRрқҗҝz\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{L}, вҖ–zвҖ–2вүӨвҖ–zвҖ–1вүӨвҖ–zвҖ–2вҖӢLsubscriptnormрқ‘§2subscriptnormрқ‘§1subscriptnormрқ‘§2рқҗҝ\|z\|\_{2}\leq\|z\|\_{1}\leq\|z\|\_{2}\sqrt{L}.
This also implies the last inequality of the theorem statement.
The failure probabilities of CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") for the diagonal terms, and LemmaВ [34](#Thmtheorem34 "Lemma 34. вҖЈ 4.2 Rotations for Encoding Sequences вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") for the off-diagonal terms, imply the overall bound via a union bound.
The last line follows using LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
вҲҺ

##### 4.2.1 Tighter Bounds for Characteristic Vectors

The above theorem applies to any sequence of vectors, but better bounds are obtainable for characteristic vectors, in some cases: consider vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw the characteristic vectors of distinct symbols.
Then SВҜвҖӢvВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}v and RвҖӢSВҜвҖӢwрқ‘…ВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘ӨR{\bar{S}}w are entry-wise independent, because vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw select different columns of SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}}, and the rotation RвҖӢSВҜрқ‘…ВҜрқ‘ҶR{\bar{S}} doesnвҖҷt change this.
Next we apply this idea more generally.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [10](#Thmtheorem10 "Theorem 10. вҖЈ Rotations via JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Given scaled sign matrix SВҜвҲҲIвҖӢRmГ—dВҜрқ‘ҶsuperscriptIRрқ‘ҡрқ‘‘{\bar{S}}\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{m\times d}, rotation matrix RвҲҲIвҖӢRmГ—mрқ‘…superscriptIRрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҡR\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{m\times m} (Def.В [7](#Thmtheorem7 "Definition 7. вҖЈ Rotations via JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), integer L>0рқҗҝ0L>0, and SВҜR,LsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘…рқҗҝ{\bar{S}}\_{R,L} as in Def.В [8](#Thmtheorem8 "Definition 8. вҖЈ Rotations via JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
For a sequence of vectors v(0),v(1),вҖҰвҖӢv(LвҲ’1)вҲҲ{0,1}d

subscriptрқ‘Ј0subscriptрқ‘Ј1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Јрқҗҝ1
superscript01рқ‘‘v\_{(0)},v\_{(1)},\ldots v\_{(L-1)}\in\{0,1\}^{d}, let
KвүЎвҖ–вҲ‘0вүӨj<Lv(j)вҖ–вҲһрқҗҫsubscriptnormsubscript0рқ‘—рқҗҝsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—K\equiv\|\sum\_{0\leq j<L}v\_{(j)}\|\_{\infty}.

|  |  |  |

Bounds for set difference and intersection follow by slight variation of CorollariesВ [4](#Thmtheorem4 "Corollary 4. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") and [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

##### Proof.

Our proof of this lemma uses a corollary of McDiarmidвҖҷs Inequality (Theorem [25](#Thmtheorem25 "Theorem 25. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
The product SВҜR,LвҖӢvsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘…рқҗҝрқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}\_{R,L}v is a sum of vectors of the form RjвҖӢSВҜвҲ—isuperscriptрқ‘…рқ‘—subscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘–R^{j}{\bar{S}}\_{\*i}, for entries iрқ‘–i of v(j)subscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—v\_{(j)} equal to one.

(As is not hard to verify.)

and the theorem follows, after folding KрқҗҫK into ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon} and adjusting constants.

#### 4.3 Binding

##### 4.3.1 Bundles of pair-wise bindings

As discussed in the introduction, a bundle of pairwise bindings can be given as a vector SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v, where
vвҲҲ{0,1}(d2)рқ‘Јsuperscript01binomialрқ‘‘2v\in\{0,1\}^{\binom{d}{2}}, and SВҜвҠҷ2вҲҲ{Вұ1m}mГ—(d2)superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҡbinomialрқ‘‘2{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}\in\{\pm\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\}^{m\times\binom{d}{2}} is defined in Def.В [11](#Thmtheorem11 "Definition 11. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
We have
рқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2]=вҖ–vвҖ–2рқ”јdelimited-[]superscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2superscriptnormрқ‘Ј2{\mathbb{E}}[\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}]=\|v\|^{2}, and need to show that
вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2вҲҲвҖ–vвҖ–2вҖӢ(1ВұОө)superscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2superscriptnormрқ‘Ј2plus-or-minus1рқңҖ\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}\in\|v\|^{2}(1\pm{\varepsilon}) with high probability.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

For vвҲҲ{0,1}(d2)рқ‘Јsuperscript01binomialрқ‘‘2v\in\{0,1\}^{\binom{d}{2}}, there is m=OвҖӢ(ОөвҲ’2вҖӢlog3вҒЎ(вҖ–vвҖ–1/ОөвҖӢОҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘ӮsuperscriptрқңҖ2superscript3subscriptnormрқ‘Ј1рқңҖрқӣҝm=O({\varepsilon}^{-2}\log^{3}(\|v\|\_{1}/{\varepsilon}\delta)) so that
for SВҜвҠҷ2вҲҲ{Вұ1m}(d2)superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡbinomialрқ‘‘2{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}\in\{\pm\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\}^{\binom{d}{2}},

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2вҲ’вҖ–vвҖ–2|>ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2]вүӨОҙ.PrsuperscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2superscriptnormрқ‘Ј2рқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј2рқӣҝ\Pr[|\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}-\|v\|^{2}|>{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}]\leq\delta. |  |

For our analysis we will use a graph GвҖӢ(V,E)рқҗәрқ‘үрқҗёG(V,E) of interactions in SВҜвҠҷksuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}^{\odot k} of columns in SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}}.
Index the columns of SВҜвҠҷksuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}^{\odot k} by the columns of SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}} from which they came, so SВҜвҲ—,{i1,i2,вҖҰ,ik}вҠҷksubscriptsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳ

subscriptрқ‘–1subscriptрқ‘–2вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘–рқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}\_{\*,\{i\_{1},i\_{2},\ldots,i\_{k}\}} denotes the column of SВҜвҠҷksuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}^{\odot k} that is the binding of columns SВҜвҲ—,i1,SВҜвҲ—,i2,вҖҰвҖӢSВҜвҲ—,ik

subscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ

subscriptрқ‘–1subscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ

subscriptрқ‘–2вҖҰsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ

subscriptрқ‘–рқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}\_{\*,i\_{1}},{\bar{S}}\_{\*,i\_{2}},\ldots{\bar{S}}\_{\*,i\_{k}} of SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}}.
Also use this indexing scheme for vвҲҲв„қ(dk)рқ‘Јsuperscriptв„қbinomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳv\in{\mathbb{R}}^{\binom{d}{k}}.
Now for given vвҲҲв„қ(dk)рқ‘Јsuperscriptв„қbinomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳv\in{\mathbb{R}}^{\binom{d}{k}}, the graph (or hyper-graph, for k>2рқ‘ҳ2k>2) GрқҗәG has
edges E={eвҠӮ[(dk)]вҲЈveвү 0}рқҗёconditional-setрқ‘’delimited-[]binomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘’0E=\{e\subset[\binom{d}{k}]\mid v\_{e}\neq 0\}, and
vertices V={iвҲЈiвҲҲeвҲҲE}рқ‘үconditional-setрқ‘–рқ‘–рқ‘’рқҗёV=\{i\mid i\in e\in E\}.

We can also include singleton atomic vectors in the bundling, by including the all-ones vector 1вҶ’msubscriptвҶ’1рқ‘ҡ\vec{1}\_{m} as an atomic vector, bound to each singleton.
Note that approximate orthogonality holds also for these bindings, and the dimension is (d+12)binomialрқ‘‘12\binom{d+1}{2}, within a constant factor of (d2)binomialрқ‘‘2\binom{d}{2}.

We prove TheoremВ [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") using this graphical view of SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v in the following way.
For given в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m] we can write the Rademacher variables contributing to nonzero summands of SВҜв„“вҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷв„“direct-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}\_{\ell}^{\odot 2}v as
Xв„“=(x1,x2,вҖҰ,x|V|)subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1subscriptрқ‘Ҙ2вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘үX\_{\ell}=(x\_{1},x\_{2},\ldots,x\_{|V|}), for Vрқ‘үV the vertex set of the associated graph GрқҗәG.
Also, we can express SВҜв„“вҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷв„“direct-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}\_{\ell}^{\odot 2}v as a function

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mвӢ…SВҜв„“,вҲ—вҠҷ2вҖӢv=fвҖӢ(Xв„“),whereвҖӢfвҖӢ(x)=вҲ‘{i,j}вҲҲExiвҖӢxj.formulae-sequenceвӢ…рқ‘ҡsuperscriptsubscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷ  в„“direct-productabsent2рқ‘Јрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“whereрқ‘“рқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘–рқ‘—рқҗёsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—\sqrt{m}\cdot{\bar{S}}\_{\ell,\*}^{\odot 2}v=f(X\_{\ell}),\mathrm{\ where\ }f(x)=\sum\_{\{i,j\}\in E}x\_{i}x\_{j}. |  | (1) |

##### Proof of Theorem [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

For iвҲҲ[|V|]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘үi\in[|V|], let function giвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,x|V|)subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘үg\_{i}(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{|V|}) take value xiвҖӢ(1{i}вҲҲE+вҲ‘j:(i,j)вҲҲExj)subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscript1рқ‘–рқҗёsubscript:рқ‘—рқ‘–рқ‘—рқҗёsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—x\_{i}(1\_{\{i\}\in E}+\sum\_{j:\,(i,j)\in E}x\_{j}).
(Here 1{i}вҲҲEsubscript1рқ‘–рқҗё1\_{\{i\}\in E} equals one when {i}вҲҲEрқ‘–рқҗё\{i\}\in E, and zero otherwise.)
Then, for any в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m], flipping the sign of xisubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x\_{i} changes any fвҖӢ(Xв„“)рқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“f(X\_{\ell}) by no more than 2вҖӢ|giвҖӢ(Xв„“)|2subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“2|g\_{i}(X\_{\ell})|.
By Theorem [29](#Thmtheorem29 "Theorem 29. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), with a1,вҖҰ,adegGвҒЎ(i)=1

subscriptрқ‘Һ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Һsubscriptdegreeрқҗәрқ‘–
1a\_{1},\ldots,a\_{\deg\_{G}(i)}=1 and t=6вҖӢlogвҒЎ(|E|вҖӢm/Оҙ)рқ‘Ў6рқҗёрқ‘ҡрқӣҝt=\sqrt{6\log(|E|m/\delta)}, we have

|  |  |  |  |

|  | PrвҒЎ[2вҖӢ|giвҖӢ(Xв„“)|>2вҖӢ6вҖӢdegGвҒЎ(i)вӢ…logвҒЎ(2вҖӢ|E|вҖӢm/Оҙ)]<Оҙ38вҖӢ|E|3вҖӢm3.Pr2subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“2вӢ…6subscriptdegreeрқҗәрқ‘–2рқҗёрқ‘ҡрқӣҝsuperscriptрқӣҝ38superscriptрқҗё3superscriptрқ‘ҡ3\Pr\left[2|g\_{i}(X\_{\ell})|>2\sqrt{6\deg\_{G}(i)\cdot\log(2|E|m/\delta)}\right]<\frac{\delta^{3}}{8|E|^{3}m^{3}}. |  | (2) |

|  |  |  |

noting that 2вҖӢ|E|вүҘ|V|2рқҗёрқ‘ү2|E|\geq|V|, since each vertex occurs in some edge, and at most two vertices occur in one edge.

For в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m], let function fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell}) be equal to fвҖӢ(Xв„“)рқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“f(X\_{\ell}) when в„°в„°{\mathcal{E}} holds, and be zero otherwise.
By McDiarmidвҖҷs Inequality, TheoremВ [25](#Thmtheorem25 "Theorem 25. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"),

From PropositionВ 2.5.2 of [vershynin\_high-dimensional\_2018], therefore, for all в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m], fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})] is a sub-Gaussian random variable, with proxy variance within a constant factor of at most

Let fВҜвүЎрқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(X)]ВҜрқ‘“рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ\bar{f}\equiv{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X)], for Rademacher Xрқ‘ӢX.
Since рқ”јвҖӢ[fвҖӢ(X)]=0рқ”јdelimited-[]рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ0{\mathbb{E}}[f(X)]=0, we have

since |fвҖӢ(X)|вүӨ|E|рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқҗё|f(X)|\leq|E|.

Let FЛҮвүЎ1mвҖӢвҲ‘в„“fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)2ЛҮрқҗ№1рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„“ЛҮрқ‘“superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“2{\check{F}}\equiv\frac{1}{m}\sum\_{\ell}{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})^{2}, and FЛҮcвүЎ1mвҖӢвҲ‘в„“(fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҲ’fВҜ)2subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җ1рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„“superscriptЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“ВҜрқ‘“2{\check{F}}\_{c}\equiv\frac{1}{m}\sum\_{\ell}({\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})-\bar{f})^{2}.
Using ExerciseВ 2.7.10 and CorollaryВ 2.8.3 of [vershynin\_high-dimensional\_2018], it follows that

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|FЛҮcвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮc]|>t]вүӨ2вҖӢexpвҒЎ(вҲ’cвҖӢmвҖӢminвҒЎ(t2ПғfЛҮ4,tПғfЛҮ2)).PrsubscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ‘Ў2рқ‘җрқ‘ҡsuperscriptрқ‘Ў2superscriptsubscriptрқңҺЛҮрқ‘“4рқ‘ЎsuperscriptsubscriptрқңҺЛҮрқ‘“2\displaystyle\Pr[|{\check{F}}\_{c}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}\_{c}]|>t]\leq 2\exp\left(-cm\min\left(\frac{t^{2}}{\sigma\_{\check{f}}^{4}},\frac{t}{\sigma\_{\check{f}}^{2}}\right)\right). |  |

2exp(вҲ’cmОө2/log(|E|m/Оҙ)2)2\exp(-cm{\varepsilon}^{2}/\log(|E|m/\delta)^{2}), for a different constant cрқ‘җc, so there is m=O(ОөвҲ’2log(|E|/ОөОҙ)3)m=O({\varepsilon}^{-2}\log(|E|/{\varepsilon}\delta)^{3}) such that

|  |  |  |  |
