We have a tail estimate for FЛҮcsubscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җ{\check{F}}\_{c}, but not for FЛҮЛҮрқҗ№{\check{F}} or
вҖ–PвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2=1mвҖӢвҲ‘в„“fвҖӢ(Xв„“)2superscriptnormsuperscriptрқ‘ғdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј21рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„“рқ‘“superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“2\|P^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}=\frac{1}{m}\sum\_{\ell}f(X\_{\ell})^{2}.
We have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | FЛҮcвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮc]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җ\displaystyle{\check{F}}\_{c}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}\_{c}] | =1mвҖӢвҲ‘в„“(fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҲ’fВҜ)2вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“вҲ’fВҜ)2]absent1рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„“superscriptЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“ВҜрқ‘“2рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“ВҜрқ‘“2\displaystyle=\frac{1}{m}\sum\_{\ell}({\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})-\bar{f})^{2}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell}-\bar{f})^{2}] |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =FЛҮвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮ]+1mвҖӢвҲ‘в„“вҲ’2вҖӢfЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҖӢfВҜ+fВҜ2+2вҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҖӢfВҜ]вҲ’fВҜ2absentЛҮрқҗ№рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқҗ№1рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„“2ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“ВҜрқ‘“superscriptВҜрқ‘“22рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“ВҜрқ‘“superscriptВҜрқ‘“2\displaystyle={\check{F}}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}]+\frac{1}{m}\sum\_{\ell}-2{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})\bar{f}+\bar{f}^{2}+2{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})\bar{f}]-\bar{f}^{2} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =FЛҮвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮ]+2вҖӢfВҜ2вҲ’2mвҖӢfВҜвҖӢвҲ‘в„“fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“).absentЛҮрқҗ№рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқҗ№2superscriptВҜрқ‘“22рқ‘ҡВҜрқ‘“subscriptв„“ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“\displaystyle={\check{F}}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}]+2\bar{f}^{2}-\frac{2}{m}\bar{f}\sum\_{\ell}{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell}). |  |

Using ([3](#S4.E3 "In Proof of Theorem 12. вҖЈ 4.3.1 Bundles of pair-wise bindings вҖЈ 4.3 Binding вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and |fвҖӢ(X)|вүӨ|E|рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣрқҗё|f(X)|\leq|E|, we have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | |FЛҮвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮ]|вүӨ|FЛҮcвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮc]|+4вҖӢОҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2.ЛҮрқҗ№рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқҗ№subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җ4subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё2|{\check{F}}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}]|\leq|{\check{F}}\_{c}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}\_{c}]|+4\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2}. |  | (5) |

We can apply LemmaВ [26](#Thmtheorem26 "Lemma 26. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") to SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v and FЛҮЛҮрқҗ№{\check{F}}, as fрқ‘“f and gрқ‘”g in that lemma, using that FЛҮ=вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2ЛҮрқҗ№superscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2{\check{F}}=\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2} with failure probability at most Оҙв„°subscriptрқӣҝв„°\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}, and that вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2вүӨ|E|2superscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2superscriptрқҗё2\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}\leq|E|^{2}.
Using t=ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2/2+4вҖӢОҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2рқ‘ЎрқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј224subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё2t={\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}/2+4\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2} in that lemma, together with ([5](#S4.E5 "In Proof of Theorem 12. вҖЈ 4.3.1 Bundles of pair-wise bindings вҖЈ 4.3 Binding вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and ([4](#S4.E4 "In Proof of Theorem 12. вҖЈ 4.3.1 Bundles of pair-wise bindings вҖЈ 4.3 Binding вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), we have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|вҖ–SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҖ–2вҲ’вҖ–vвҖ–2|>ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2/2+4вҖӢОҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2+Оҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2]PrsuperscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј2superscriptnormрқ‘Ј2рқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј224subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё2subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё2\displaystyle\Pr[|\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v\|^{2}-\|v\|^{2}|>{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}/2+4\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2}+\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2}] | вүӨPrвҒЎ[|FЛҮвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮ]|>ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2/2+4вҖӢОҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2]absentPrЛҮрқҗ№рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқҗ№рқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј224subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё2\displaystyle\leq\Pr[|{\check{F}}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}]|>{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}/2+4\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2}] |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨPrвҒЎ[|FЛҮcвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮc]|>ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2/2]+Оҙв„°absentPrsubscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј22subscriptрқӣҝв„°\displaystyle\leq\Pr[|{\check{F}}\_{c}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}\_{c}]|>{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}/2]+\delta\_{\mathcal{E}} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨОҙ/2+Оҙв„°вүӨОҙ.absentрқӣҝ2subscriptрқӣҝв„°рқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\delta/2+\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}\leq\delta. |  |

The theorem follows, using 5вҖӢОҙв„°вҖӢ|E|2=5вҖӢОҙ3/4вҖӢm2<ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2/25subscriptрқӣҝв„°superscriptрқҗё25superscriptрқӣҝ34superscriptрқ‘ҡ2рқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј225\delta\_{\mathcal{E}}|E|^{2}=5\delta^{3}/4m^{2}<{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}/2, possibly adjusting mрқ‘ҡm by a constant factor.

вҲҺ

##### 4.3.2 Bundles of Bindings of Multiple Vectors

We can again hope to use Corollary [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") in this setting.
However, to obtain the appropriate constants c1,вҖҰ,cn

subscriptрқ‘җ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘ӣc\_{1},\ldots,c\_{n} to use in Corollary [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we cannot directly apply TheoremВ [29](#Thmtheorem29 "Theorem 29. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"); it is only a base case, for when k=2рқ‘ҳ2k=2.
We proceed via induction on the maximum binding size.

##### Lemma 36.

Given hypergraph G=(V,E)рқҗәрқ‘үрқҗёG=(V,E), let fвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,x|V|)=вҲ‘eвҲҲEвҲҸiвҲҲexiрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘үsubscriptрқ‘’рқҗёsubscriptproductрқ‘–рқ‘’subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–f(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{|V|})=\sum\_{e\in E}\prod\_{i\in e}x\_{i}, and let kрқ‘ҳk be the maximum hyperedge size.
Let X=(X1,вҖҰ,X|V|)рқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ӣ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘үX=(X\_{1},\ldots,X\_{|V|}) be a tuple of independent random Rademacher variables, i.e., each takes values {Вұ1}plus-or-minus1\{\pm 1\} with probability 1212\frac{1}{2}.
For Оҙ0вүӨOвҖӢ(1/|E|)subscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘Ӯ1рқҗё\delta\_{0}\leq O\left(1/\sqrt{|E|}\right):

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|fвҖӢ(X)|вүҘ2вҖӢk!вӢ…|E|вҖӢlogk/2вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)]Prрқ‘“рқ‘Ӣ2вӢ…рқ‘ҳрқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0\displaystyle\Pr\left[|f(X)|\geq 2\sqrt{k!\cdot|E|}\log^{k/2}\left(k/\delta\_{0}\right)\right] | вүӨОҙ0absentsubscriptрқӣҝ0\displaystyle\leq\delta\_{0} |  |

##### Proof.

We proceed by induction on kрқ‘ҳk.
When k=2рқ‘ҳ2k=2, we are done by TheoremВ [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

To handle general kрқ‘ҳk, we again apply the version of McDiarmid in Corollary [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
If we fix (x1,вҖҰ,x|V|)subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘ү(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{|V|}), changing the value of xisubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x\_{i} again changes fрқ‘“f by at most вҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲEвҲҸjвҲҲE:jвү ixjsubscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқҗёsubscriptproduct:рқ‘—рқҗёрқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—\sum\_{e\in E:\,i\in E}\prod\_{j\in E:\,j\neq i}x\_{j}.
The expression вҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲEвҲҸjвҲҲE:jвү ixjsubscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқҗёsubscriptproduct:рқ‘—рқҗёрқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—\sum\_{e\in E:\,i\in E}\prod\_{j\in E:\,j\neq i}x\_{j} encodes a hypergraph Gi=(Vi,Ei)subscriptрқҗәрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘үрқ‘–subscriptрқҗёрқ‘–G\_{i}=(V\_{i},E\_{i}) with maximum edge size kвҲ’1рқ‘ҳ1k-1, so by induction, we may assume:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|вҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲEвҲҸjвҲҲE:jвү ixj|вүҘ2вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вҖӢ|Ei|вҖӢlog(kвҲ’1)/2вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)]вүӨ(kвҲ’1)вҖӢОҙ0kPrsubscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқҗёsubscriptproduct:рқ‘—рқҗёрқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—2рқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқҗёрқ‘–superscriptрқ‘ҳ12рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘ҳ\Pr\left[\left|\sum\_{e\in E:\,i\in E}\prod\_{j\in E:\,j\neq i}x\_{j}\right|\geq 2\sqrt{(k-1)!|E\_{i}|}\log^{(k-1)/2}\left(k/\delta\_{0}\right)\right]\leq\frac{(k-1)\delta\_{0}}{k} |  |

Now, we invoke Corollary [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") with ci=2вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вҖӢ|Ei|вҖӢlog(kвҲ’1)/2вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)subscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2рқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқҗёрқ‘–superscriptрқ‘ҳ12рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0c\_{i}=2\sqrt{(k-1)!|E\_{i}|}\log^{(k-1)/2}(k/\delta\_{0}).

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | вҲ‘i=1|V|ci2superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘үsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2\displaystyle\sum\_{i=1}^{|V|}c\_{i}^{2} | =вҲ‘i=1|V|4вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вҖӢ|Ei|вҖӢlogkвҲ’1вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)absentsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘ү4рқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқҗёрқ‘–superscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0\displaystyle=\sum\_{i=1}^{|V|}4(k-1)!|E\_{i}|\log^{k-1}(k/\delta\_{0}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =4вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вҖӢlogkвҲ’1вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)вҖӢвҲ‘i=1|V||Ei|absent4рқ‘ҳ1superscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘үsubscriptрқҗёрқ‘–\displaystyle=4(k-1)!\log^{k-1}(k/\delta\_{0})\sum\_{i=1}^{|V|}|E\_{i}| |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨ4вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вҖӢ(logkвҲ’1вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0))вӢ…kвҖӢ|E|absentвӢ…4рқ‘ҳ1superscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘ҳрқҗё\displaystyle\leq 4(k-1)!(\log^{k-1}(k/\delta\_{0}))\cdot k|E| |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =4вҖӢk!вӢ…|E|вҖӢlogkвҲ’1вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)absentвӢ…4рқ‘ҳрқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0\displaystyle=4k!\cdot|E|\log^{k-1}(k/\delta\_{0}) |  |

We can also set t=2вҖӢk!вӢ…|E|вҖӢlogk/2вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)рқ‘Ў2вӢ…рқ‘ҳрқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0t=\sqrt{2}\sqrt{k!\cdot|E|}\log^{k/2}(k/\delta\_{0}). Then,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | t2=2вҖӢk!вӢ…|E|вҖӢlogkвҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)вүҘ12вҖӢlogвҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)вҖӢвҲ‘i=1|V|ci2superscriptрқ‘Ў2вӢ…2рқ‘ҳрқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ012рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0superscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1рқ‘үsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘җрқ‘–2t^{2}=2k!\cdot|E|\log^{k}(k/\delta\_{0})\geq\frac{1}{2}\log(k/\delta\_{0})\sum\_{i=1}^{|V|}c\_{i}^{2} |  |

Finally, setting Оҙ=(kвҲ’1)вҖӢОҙ0kрқӣҝрқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘ҳ\delta=\frac{(k-1)\delta\_{0}}{k}, M=|E|рқ‘ҖрқҗёM=|E|, Corollary [27](#Thmtheorem27 "Corollary 27. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") implies:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Pr[|f(X)]|вүҘ2k!вӢ…|E|logk/2(k/Оҙ0)+(kвҲ’1)вӢ…|E|вӢ…Оҙ0k]вүӨОҙ0k+(kвҲ’1)вҖӢОҙ0kвүӨОҙ0\Pr\left[\left|f(X)]\right|\geq\sqrt{2}\sqrt{k!\cdot|E|}\log^{k/2}(k/\delta\_{0})+\frac{(k-1)\cdot|E|\cdot\delta\_{0}}{k}\right]\leq\frac{\delta\_{0}}{k}+\frac{(k-1)\delta\_{0}}{k}\leq\delta\_{0} |  |

To complete the proof, it suffices to show

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | (kвҲ’1)вӢ…|E|вӢ…Оҙ0kвүӨ(2вҲ’2)вҖӢk!вӢ…|E|вҖӢlogk/2вҒЎ(k/Оҙ0)вӢ…рқ‘ҳ1рқҗёsubscriptрқӣҝ0рқ‘ҳ22вӢ…рқ‘ҳрқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқӣҝ0\frac{(k-1)\cdot|E|\cdot\delta\_{0}}{k}\leq(2-\sqrt{2})\sqrt{k!\cdot|E|}\log^{k/2}(k/\delta\_{0}) |  |

However, given our upper bound on Оҙ0subscriptрқӣҝ0\delta\_{0}, this holds for all values of kрқ‘ҳk.
вҲҺ

##### Corollary (Restatement of Corollary [13](#Thmtheorem13 "Corollary 13. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

For scaled sign SВҜвҠҷkвҲҲ{Вұ1m}(dk)superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳsuperscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡbinomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳ{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}\in\{\pm\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\}^{\binom{d}{k}}, vвҲҲ{0,1}(dk)рқ‘Јsuperscript01binomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳv\in\{0,1\}^{\binom{d}{k}}, and iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m],
there is C>0рқҗ¶0C>0 and m=OвҖӢ(ОөвҲ’2вҖӢCkвҖӢlogвҒЎkвҖӢlogk+1вҒЎ(kвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–1/(ОөвҖӢОҙ)))рқ‘ҡрқ‘ӮsuperscriptрқңҖ2superscriptрқҗ¶рқ‘ҳрқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1рқңҖрқӣҝm=O(\varepsilon^{-2}C^{k\log k}\log^{k+1}(k\|v\|\_{1}/(\varepsilon\delta))) such that

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|вҖ–SВҜвҠҷkвҖӢvвҖ–2вҲ’вҖ–vвҖ–2|>ОөвҖӢвҖ–vвҖ–2]вүӨОҙ.PrsuperscriptnormsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳрқ‘Ј2superscriptnormрқ‘Ј2рқңҖsuperscriptnormрқ‘Ј2рқӣҝ\Pr[|\|{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}v\|^{2}-\|v\|^{2}|>{\varepsilon}\|v\|^{2}]\leq\delta. |  |

Just as there was a graphical view of SВҜвҠҷ2вҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot 2}v, we have a natural way to view SВҜвҠҷkвҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳрқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}v as a hypergraph H=(V,E)рқҗ»рқ‘үрқҗёH=(V,E).
For each в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m], let Xв„“=(x1,x2,вҖҰ,x|V|)subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1subscriptрқ‘Ҙ2вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘үX\_{\ell}=(x\_{1},x\_{2},\ldots,x\_{|V|}) be the Rademacher variables contributing to the summands of SВҜв„“вҠҷk,вҲ—v{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}\_{\ell},\*v, the в„“в„“\ell-th entry of SВҜвҠҷkвҖӢvsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳрқ‘Ј{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}v, and we can write

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | fвҖӢ(Xв„“)вүЎmвҖӢSВҜв„“вҠҷk=вҲ‘(i1,вҖҰ,ik)вҲҲExi1вҖӢxi2вҖӢвӢҜвҖӢxikрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“рқ‘ҡsubscriptsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsentрқ‘ҳв„“subscriptsubscriptрқ‘–1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘–рқ‘ҳрқҗёsubscriptрқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘–1subscriptрқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘–2вӢҜsubscriptрқ‘Ҙsubscriptрқ‘–рқ‘ҳf(X\_{\ell})\equiv\sqrt{m}{\bar{S}}^{\odot k}\_{\ell}=\sum\_{(i\_{1},\ldots,i\_{k})\in E}x\_{i\_{1}}x\_{i\_{2}}\cdots x\_{i\_{k}} |  |

##### Proof.

We will follow the same approach to the proof of Theorem [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
Due to the similarity of the proofs, we will omit steps here, but we will keep track of the parameters and calculations that differ.

Fix iвҲҲ[|V|]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘үi\in[|V|], and define giвҖӢ(x1,вҖҰ,x|V|)=xiвҖӢвҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲeвҲҸjвҲҲe,jвү ixjsubscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘үsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқ‘’subscriptproductformulae-sequenceрқ‘—рқ‘’рқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—g\_{i}(x\_{1},\ldots,x\_{|V|})=x\_{i}\sum\_{e\in E:i\in e}\prod\_{j\in e,j\neq i}x\_{j}.
For each coordinate в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m], flipping the sign of xisubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x\_{i} will change fвҖӢ(Xв„“)рқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“f(X\_{\ell}) by at most вҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲeвҲҸjвҲҲe,jвү ixjsubscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқ‘’subscriptproductformulae-sequenceрқ‘—рқ‘’рқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—\sum\_{e\in E:i\in e}\prod\_{j\in e,j\neq i}x\_{j}.
Lemma [36](#Thmtheorem36 "Lemma 36. вҖЈ 4.3.2 Bundles of Bindings of Multiple Vectors вҖЈ 4.3 Binding вҖЈ 4 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") gives us a high probability bound on the magnitude of вҲ‘eвҲҲE:iвҲҲeвҲҸjвҲҲe,jвү ixjsubscript:рқ‘’рқҗёрқ‘–рқ‘’subscriptproductformulae-sequenceрқ‘—рқ‘’рқ‘—рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—\sum\_{e\in E:i\in e}\prod\_{j\in e,j\neq i}x\_{j}:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[2вҖӢ|giвҖӢ(Xв„“)|>2вҖӢ(kвҲ’1)!вӢ…3kвҲ’1вӢ…degGвҒЎ(i)вӢ…log(kвҲ’1)вҒЎ(kвҖӢ|E|вҖӢm/Оҙ)]вүӨОҙ34вҖӢkвҖӢ|E|3вҖӢm3Pr2subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“2вӢ…рқ‘ҳ1superscript3рқ‘ҳ1subscriptdegreeрқҗәрқ‘–superscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳрқҗёрқ‘ҡрқӣҝsuperscriptрқӣҝ34рқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқҗё3superscriptрқ‘ҡ3\Pr\left[2|g\_{i}(X\_{\ell})|>2\sqrt{(k-1)!\cdot 3^{k-1}\cdot\deg\_{G}(i)\cdot\log^{(k-1)}(k|E|m/\delta)}\right]\leq\frac{\delta^{3}}{4k|E|^{3}m^{3}} |  |

Choosing this upper bound on the probability ensures that we obtain the same Оҙв„°subscriptрқӣҝв„°\delta\_{\mathcal{E}} as we do in Theorem [12](#Thmtheorem12 "Theorem 12. вҖЈ Bundles of bindings the JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
Defining fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell}) as before, Theorem [25](#Thmtheorem25 "Theorem 25. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") says

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)]|вүҘt]вүӨ2вҖӢexpвҒЎ(вҲ’t2k!вӢ…3kвҲ’1вӢ…|E|вҖӢlog(kвҲ’1)вҒЎ(kвҖӢ|E|вҖӢm/Оҙ))PrЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“рқ‘Ў2superscriptрқ‘Ў2вӢ…рқ‘ҳsuperscript3рқ‘ҳ1рқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳрқҗёрқ‘ҡрқӣҝ\Pr\left[|{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})]|\geq t\right]\leq 2\exp\left(-\frac{t^{2}}{k!\cdot 3^{k-1}\cdot|E|\log^{(k-1)}(k|E|m/\delta)}\right) |  |

The proxy variance of fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[fЛҮвҖӢ(Xв„“)]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“рқ”јdelimited-[]ЛҮрқ‘“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{f}}(X\_{\ell})] is now

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ПғfЛҮ2вүЎk!вӢ…3kвҲ’1вӢ…|E|вҖӢlog(kвҲ’1)вҒЎ(kвҖӢ|E|вҖӢm/Оҙ)superscriptsubscriptрқңҺЛҮрқ‘“2вӢ…рқ‘ҳsuperscript3рқ‘ҳ1рқҗёsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳрқҗёрқ‘ҡрқӣҝ\sigma\_{{\check{f}}}^{2}\equiv k!\cdot 3^{k-1}\cdot|E|\log^{(k-1)}(k|E|m/\delta) |  |

Defining FЛҮЛҮрқҗ№{\check{F}} and FЛҮcsubscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җ{\check{F}}\_{c} the same way, and choosing large enough m=OвҖӢ(ОөвҲ’2вӢ…k!2вӢ…32вҖӢkвӢ…logk+1вҒЎ(kвҖӢ|E|/(ОөвҖӢОҙ)))рқ‘ҡрқ‘ӮвӢ…superscriptрқңҖ2superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscript32рқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘ҳрқҗёрқңҖрқӣҝm=O(\varepsilon^{-2}\cdot k!^{2}\cdot 3^{2k}\cdot\log^{k+1}(k|E|/(\varepsilon\delta))), we have

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[|FЛҮcвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[FЛҮc]|>ОөвҖӢ|E|/2]вүӨОҙ/2PrsubscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptЛҮрқҗ№рқ‘җрқңҖрқҗё2рқӣҝ2\Pr\left[|{\check{F}}\_{c}-{\mathbb{E}}[{\check{F}}\_{c}]|>\varepsilon|E|/2\right]\leq\delta/2 |  |

The remainder of the proof follows without changes after we fix the value of mрқ‘ҡm.
Regarding the dependence on kрқ‘ҳk,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | logвҒЎ(k!2вҖӢ32вҖӢk)вүӨlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢПҖвҖӢkвҖӢ(k/e)2вҖӢkвҖӢe1/6вҖӢkвҖӢ32вҖӢk)=2вҖӢkвҖӢlogвҒЎ(3вҖӢk/e)+OвҖӢ(logвҒЎk)=OвҖӢ(kвҖӢlogвҒЎk),superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscript32рқ‘ҳ2рқңӢрқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘’2рқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқ‘’16рқ‘ҳsuperscript32рқ‘ҳ2рқ‘ҳ3рқ‘ҳрқ‘’рқ‘Ӯрқ‘ҳрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ҳрқ‘ҳ\log(k!^{2}3^{2k})\leq\log(2\pi k(k/e)^{2k}e^{1/6k}3^{2k})=2k\log(3k/e)+O(\log k)=O(k\log k), |  |

using an inequality form of StirlingвҖҷs approximation. The corollary follows.
вҲҺ

### 5 Autocorrelation Associative Memories as Bundles of Robust Bindings

As discussed in В§[2.3](#S2.SS3 "2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), this section provides a new analysis of Hopfield networks, and proposes a Hopfield variant that is a space-efficient VSA bundling operation.

#### 5.1 Analysis of Hopfield Networks via Concentration Bounds

Our analysis is akin to that of [mceliece\_capacity\_1987], but uses concentration bounds instead of large deviation bounds holding in the limit.
The results are similar, in leading terms.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [14](#Thmtheorem14 "Theorem 14. вҖЈ 2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Given matrix SвҲҲ{Вұ1}mГ—nрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡрқ‘ӣS\in\{\pm 1\}^{m\times n} with uniform independent entries, jвҲҲ[n]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘ӣj\in[n], and ОҙвҲҲ(0,1]рқӣҝ01\delta\in(0,1].
If yвҲҲ{0,Вұ1}mрқ‘Ұsuperscript0plus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡy\in\{0,\pm 1\}^{m} with
yвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j/вҖ–yвҖ–вүҘ2вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)superscriptрқ‘Ұtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—normрқ‘Ұ2рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝy^{\top}S\_{\*j}/\|y\|\geq 2\sqrt{n\log(2m/\delta)}, then with failure probability at mostВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, signвүҘвҒЎ((SвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’nвҖӢIm)вҖӢy)=SвҲ—jsubscriptsignрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘ҡрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—\operatorname{{\text{sign}\_{\geq}}}((SS^{\top}-nI\_{m})y)=S\_{\*j}.
Here it is assumed that the coordinates iрқ‘–i at which yiвү SiвҖӢjsubscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘–рқ‘—y\_{i}\neq S\_{ij} are chosen beforeВ Sрқ‘ҶS, or without knowledge of it.

Since mвүҘ(yвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j)2/вҖ–yвҖ–1рқ‘ҡsuperscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ұtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—2subscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1m\geq(y^{\top}S\_{\*j})^{2}/\|y\|\_{1}, a necessary condition here is that mвүҘ4вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)рқ‘ҡ4рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝm\geq 4n\log(2m/\delta).
When y=SвҲ—jрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—y=S\_{\*j}, yвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j=m=вҖ–yвҖ–1superscriptрқ‘Ұtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—рқ‘ҡsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1y^{\top}S\_{\*j}=m=\|y\|\_{1}, and mвүҘ4вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)рқ‘ҡ4рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝm\geq 4n\log(2m/\delta) suffices.
There is

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | m=(1+oвҖӢ(1))вҖӢ4вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢn/Оҙ)вҖӢasвҖӢn/ОҙвҶ’вҲһрқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ң14рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ӣрқӣҝasрқ‘ӣрқӣҝвҶ’m=(1+o(1))4n\log(2n/\delta)\mathrm{\ as\ }n/\delta\rightarrow\infty |  |

such that mвүҘ4вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)рқ‘ҡ4рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝm\geq 4n\log(2m/\delta).

##### Proof.

Let IвҲ’jвҲҲв„қnГ—nsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘—superscriptв„қрқ‘ӣрқ‘ӣI\_{-j}\in{\mathbb{R}}^{n\times n} denote the identity matrix with its jрқ‘—jвҖҷth diagonal entry set to zero.
We have

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | (SвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’nвҖӢIm)вҖӢy=SвҲ—jвҖӢSвҲ—jвҠӨвҖӢyвҲ’y+(SвҖӢIвҲ’jвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’(nвҲ’1)вҖӢI)вҖӢy.рқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘ҡрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topрқ‘Ұрқ‘Ұрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘—superscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣ1рқҗјрқ‘Ұ(SS^{\top}-nI\_{m})y=S\_{\*j}S\_{\*j}^{\top}y-y+(SI\_{-j}S^{\top}-(n-1)I)y. |  |

The first coordinate of (SвҖӢIвҲ’jвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’(nвҲ’1)вҖӢI)вҖӢyрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘—superscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣ1рқҗјрқ‘Ұ(SI\_{-j}S^{\top}-(n-1)I)y
is вҲ‘jвҖІвҲҲ[n]jвҖІвү jвҲ‘1<jвҖІвҖІвүӨmS1вҖӢjвҖІвҖӢSjвҖІвҖӢjвҖІвҖІвҖӢyjвҖІвҖІsubscript

superscriptрқ‘—вҖІdelimited-[]рқ‘ӣsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІрқ‘—subscript1superscriptрқ‘—вҖІвҖІрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ1superscriptрқ‘—вҖІsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІвҖІsubscriptрқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘—вҖІвҖІ\sum\_{\begin{subarray}{c}j^{\prime}\in[n]\\
j^{\prime}\neq j\end{subarray}}\sum\_{1<j^{\prime\prime}\leq m}S\_{1j^{\prime}}S\_{j^{\prime}j^{\prime\prime}}y\_{j^{\prime\prime}},
which is a sum of at most (nвҲ’1)вҖӢ(вҖ–yвҖ–1вҲ’1)вүӨnвҖӢвҖ–yвҖ–1рқ‘ӣ1subscriptnormрқ‘Ұ11рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1(n-1)(\|y\|\_{1}-1)\leq n\|y\|\_{1} independent Вұ1plus-or-minus1\pm 1 values.
By TheoremВ [29](#Thmtheorem29 "Theorem 29. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), with failure probability at most 2вҖӢexpвҒЎ(вҲ’Оұ)2рқӣј2\exp(-\alpha), this sum is bounded by
2вҖӢОұвҖӢnвҖӢвҖ–yвҖ–12рқӣјрқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1\sqrt{2\alpha n\|y\|\_{1}} in magnitude.
For Оұ=logвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)рқӣј2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝ\alpha=\log(2m/\delta), with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, every coordinate of (SвҖӢIвҲ’jвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’(nвҲ’1)вҖӢI)вҖӢyрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘—superscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣ1рқҗјрқ‘Ұ(SI\_{-j}S^{\top}-(n-1)I)y is at most 2вҖӢОұвҖӢnвҖӢвҖ–yвҖ–12рқӣјрқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1\sqrt{2\alpha n\|y\|\_{1}}.

Assuming this bound, if
SвҲ—jвҠӨвҖӢyвҲ’1>2вҖӢОұвҖӢnвҖӢвҖ–yвҖ–1superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topрқ‘Ұ12рқӣјрқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ1S\_{\*j}^{\top}y-1>\sqrt{2\alpha n\|y\|\_{1}},
then SiвҖӢjвҖӢSвҲ—jвҠӨвҖӢyвҲ’yisubscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘–рқ‘—superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘–S\_{ij}S\_{\*j}^{\top}y-y\_{i} agree in sign with SiвҖӢjsubscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘–рқ‘—S\_{ij}, and will exceed ((SвҖӢIвҲ’jвҖӢSвҠӨвҲ’(nвҲ’1)вҖӢI)вҖӢy)isubscriptрқ‘Ҷsubscriptрқҗјрқ‘—superscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘ӣ1рқҗјрқ‘Ұрқ‘–((SI\_{-j}S^{\top}-(n-1)I)y)\_{i} in magnitude, for all iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m], and therefore signвүҘвҒЎ(SвҖӢSвҠӨвҖӢy)=SвҲ—jsubscriptsignрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—\operatorname{{\text{sign}\_{\geq}}}(SS^{\top}y)=S\_{\*j}.
For this it is enough if SвҲ—jвҠӨвҖӢy/вҖ–yвҖ–1>2вҖӢОұвҖӢn=2вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topрқ‘Ұsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ12рқӣјрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝS\_{\*j}^{\top}y/\sqrt{\|y\|\_{1}}>2\sqrt{\alpha n}=2\sqrt{n\log(2m/\delta)}, as claimed.
вҲҺ

##### Relation to VSA: bundling of bindings

Suppose mрқ‘ҡm is even, and we can write SвҲ—j=[xy]subscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘Ҙрқ‘ҰS\_{\*j}=\left[\begin{smallmatrix}x\\
y\end{smallmatrix}\right], for x,yвҲҲ{Вұ1}m/2

рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ
superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡ2x,y\in\{\pm 1\}^{m/2}.
Then assuming the above conditions, there is m=OвҖӢ(nвҖӢlogвҒЎ(n/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ӣрқ‘ӣрқӣҝm=O(n\log(n/\delta)) so that the Hopfield output on input [x0]delimited-[]рқ‘Ҙ0\left[\begin{smallmatrix}x\\
0\end{smallmatrix}\right] or [0y]delimited-[]0рқ‘Ұ\left[\begin{smallmatrix}0\\
y\end{smallmatrix}\right] will be SвҲ—jsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—S\_{\*j}.
In this special case, the Hopfield network does a bit more than a bundle of pairwise bindings can do: it returns the other vector of a binding, without performing membership tests over a dictionary of vectors (cleanup).
This should not be entirely surprising, since
[xy]вҖӢ[xy]вҠӨ=[xвҖӢxвҠӨxвҖӢyвҠӨyвҖӢxвҠӨyвҖӢyвҠӨ]delimited-[]рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұsuperscriptdelimited-[]рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұtopdelimited-[]рқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ұtopрқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopрқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘Ұtop\left[\begin{smallmatrix}x\\
y\end{smallmatrix}\right]\left[\begin{smallmatrix}x\\
y\end{smallmatrix}\right]^{\top}=\left[\begin{smallmatrix}xx^{\top}&xy^{\top}\\
yx^{\top}&yy^{\top}\end{smallmatrix}\right], and the diagonal entries of xвҖӢyвҠӨрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ұtopxy^{\top} and yвҖӢxвҠӨрқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopyx^{\top} form the Hadamard product vector (i.e. element-wise product vector) xвҲҳyрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұx\circ y, which is the MAP-I binding of xрқ‘Ҙx and yрқ‘Ұy.

Looking at the weight matrix W=вҲ‘j=1nSвҲ—jвҖӢSвҲ—jвҠӨрқ‘Ҡsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘—1рқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—superscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topW=\sum\_{j=1}^{n}S\_{\*j}S\_{\*j}^{\top}, the two particular diagonals observed above contain exactly the MAP-I bundling of pairwise bindings of MAP-I atomic vectors, of dimension equal to half the net size.
Also, the outer product xвҖӢyвҠӨрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ұtopxy^{\top} is the binding operator for xрқ‘Ҙx and yрқ‘Ұy proposed by [smolensky\_tensor\_1990], and the relation of this binding operator to the MAP-I binding as a reduced representation is well-known via [frady\_variable\_2021].

As mentioned in the introduction, much of this discussion, including the weight matrix as a sum of outer products of the input vectors, the fixed-point condition for representation, the mapping to neural networks, and reconstruction from erasures, goes back at least to [nakano\_associatron-model\_1972, kohonen\_correlation\_1972, anderson\_simple\_1972].

##### Thinning the weight matrix

By TheoremВ [14](#Thmtheorem14 "Theorem 14. вҖЈ 2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), it suffices if вҖ–yвҖ–1вүҘ2вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)subscriptnormрқ‘Ұ12рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝ\|y\|\_{1}\geq 2n\log(2m/\delta) for the theoremвҖҷs conclusion to apply, so that the SвҲ—jsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—S\_{\*j} matching yрқ‘Ұy can be reconstructed.
That is, for diagonal matrix VвҲҲ{0,1}mГ—mрқ‘үsuperscript01рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҡV\in\{0,1\}^{m\times m}, if вҖ–VвҖӢyвҖ–1вүҘ2вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)subscriptnormрқ‘үрқ‘Ұ12рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝ\|Vy\|\_{1}\geq 2n\log(2m/\delta) is large enough, signвүҘвҒЎ(SвҖӢSвҠӨвҖӢVвҖӢy)=SвҲ—jsubscriptsignрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘үрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—\operatorname{{\text{sign}\_{\geq}}}(SS^{\top}Vy)=S\_{\*j}.
We could regard this, for given V,y

рқ‘үрқ‘ҰV,y, as signвүҘвҒЎ(WвҖӢy)subscriptsignрқ‘Ҡрқ‘Ұ\operatorname{{\text{sign}\_{\geq}}}(Wy) for a matrix WвүЎSвҖӢSвҠӨвҖӢVрқ‘Ҡрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷtopрқ‘үW\equiv SS^{\top}V with вҖ–VвҖ–F2superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘үрқҗ№2\|V\|\_{F}^{2} nonzero columns: we erase columns of SвҖӢSвҠӨрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘ҶtopSS^{\top}, not entries ofВ yрқ‘Ұy.
That is, if nрқ‘ӣn vectors are to be stored, but the vector dimension is fixed at larger than mвү«2вҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢm/Оҙ)much-greater-thanрқ‘ҡ2рқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡрқӣҝm\gg 2n\log(2m/\delta), the necessary number of stored entries is smaller than m2superscriptрқ‘ҡ2m^{2}.

##### VSAs, Autocorrelation Associative Memories, and modern Hopfield nets.

A different neural network model was proposed in recent years by [krotov\_dense\_2016], sometimes called a *modern* Hopfield network, which also uses a dynamic process to produce its output.
Here the output of an iteration is more вҖңpeaked;вҖқ for example, a version by [demircigil\_model\_2017] uses softmax when computing the next iterate.
This model has a higher capacity than classical associative memories using sums of outer products.
However, it stores all its input vectors explicitly, so that the main question is not whether the given vectors are *represented* (since they are stored), but under what circumstances the dynamic process *converges*.
The number of entries stored in this model is ОҳвҖӢ(mвҖӢn)Оҳрқ‘ҡрқ‘ӣ\Theta(mn), where (classic) associative networks store ОҳвҖӢ(m2)Оҳsuperscriptрқ‘ҡ2\Theta(m^{2}), and VSAs store ОҳвҖӢ(m)Оҳрқ‘ҡ\Theta(m).
The different amounts of storage imply different capabilities:

* вҖў

  The modern Hopfield model gives a high-capacity way to do maximum inner product search on a set of vectors, using a neural network formalism.
* вҖў

  The associatron/original Hopfield model supports the reconstruction of a vector in a stored set of vectors from an erased or noisy version.
* вҖў

  VSAs support membership tests, telling us whether two given vectors are present as a bound pair in a set.

#### 5.2 HopfieldВұplus-or-minus\pm: Autocorrelation Associative Memories as VSAs

We can also use an AAM/Hopfield model (a sum of vector outer products) to do set intersection estimation, as in VSAs.
Here we represent a bundle as the sum of outer products of a vector with itself, as in [smolensky\_tensor\_1990]. The key theorem, proven below, is the following.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [15](#Thmtheorem15 "Theorem 15. вҖЈ 2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Given Оө,ОҙвҲҲ(0,1]

рқңҖрқӣҝ
01{\varepsilon},\delta\in(0,1], scaled sign matrix SВҜвҲҲ1mвҖӢ{Вұ1}mГ—dВҜрқ‘Ҷ1рқ‘ҡsuperscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡрқ‘‘{\bar{S}}\in\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\{\pm 1\}^{m\times d} with uniform independent entries, diagonal matrix VвҲҲв„қdГ—dрқ‘үsuperscriptв„қрқ‘‘рқ‘‘V\in{\mathbb{R}}^{d\times d}, and diagonal matrix DвҲҲ{0,Вұ1}dГ—dрқҗ·superscript0plus-or-minus1рқ‘‘рқ‘‘D\in\{0,\pm 1\}^{d\times d} with uniform independent Вұ1plus-or-minus1\pm 1 diagonal entries.
There is m=O(ОөвҲ’1log(d/Оҙ)2)m=O({\varepsilon}^{-1}\log(d/\delta)^{2}) such that with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta,
вҖ–SВҜвҖӢVвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨвҖ–F2=(1ВұОө)вҖӢвҖ–VвҖ–F2superscriptsubscriptnormВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘үрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtopрқҗ№2plus-or-minus1рқңҖsuperscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘үрқҗ№2\|{\bar{S}}VD{\bar{S}}^{\top}\|\_{F}^{2}=(1\pm{\varepsilon})\|V\|\_{F}^{2}.

Since SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}} is a JL projection matrix, it will, with high probability, preserve the norms of the columns ofВ Vрқ‘үV, and multiplying by SВҜвҠӨsuperscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtop{\bar{S}}^{\top} on the right will preserve the norms of the rows of SВҜвҖӢVВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘ү{\bar{S}}V.
We can think of this as SВҜВҜрқ‘Ҷ{\bar{S}} satisfying the JL property with respect to the operation SВҜвҖӢVвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘үрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtop{\bar{S}}VD{\bar{S}}^{\top}.
The novelty here is that the dependence of mрқ‘ҡm on ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon} is ОөвҲ’1superscriptрқңҖ1{\varepsilon}^{-1}, not ОөвҲ’2superscriptрқңҖ2{\varepsilon}^{-2}; on the other hand, SВҜвҖӢVвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘үрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtop{\bar{S}}VD{\bar{S}}^{\top} comprises m2superscriptрқ‘ҡ2m^{2} values, notВ mрқ‘ҡm.
This is yet another route to preserving the norm of a vector, stored as the diagonal of Vрқ‘үV, using the same storage and speed of computation (up to log factors) as that of simply using a larger projection matrix on one side, as in MAP-I.
In other words, we obtain a bundling operator with performance characteristics similar to those of MAP-I, but using fewer random bits.

This theorem is analogous to LemmaВ [3](#Thmtheorem3 "Lemma 3 ([johnson_extensions_1984, achlioptas_database-friendly_2003], JL). вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
The following is analogous to CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), and can be proven in exactly the same way.
It implies in particular that for diagonal matrices X,Y

рқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҢX,Y representing sets, with 0/1 diagonal entries encoding element membership, the size of their intersection can be estimated accurately using their вҖңHopfield netвҖқ representations.

We have a direct analog of CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), stated below. Analogs of CorollaryВ [4](#Thmtheorem4 "Corollary 4. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") and TheoremВ [6](#Thmtheorem6 "Theorem 6. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") also follow directly; we omit the proofs.

##### Corollary 37.

Under the conditions of TheoremВ [15](#Thmtheorem15 "Theorem 15. вҖЈ 2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") (the JL property for SВҜвҖӢVвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘үрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtop{\bar{S}}VD{\bar{S}}^{\top}), for diagonal X,YвҲҲIвҖӢRdГ—d

рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң
superscriptIRрқ‘‘рқ‘‘X,Y\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{d\times d}, there is m=O(ОөвҲ’2log(d/Оҙ)2)m=O({\varepsilon}^{-2}\log(d/\delta)^{2}) so that
trвҒЎ((SВҜвҖӢXвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨ)вҖӢ(SВҜвҖӢYвҖӢDвҖӢSВҜвҠӨ))=trвҒЎ(XвҖӢY)ВұПөвҖӢвҖ–XвҖ–FвҖӢвҖ–YвҖ–FtrВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ӣрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘ҶtopВҜрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ңрқҗ·superscriptВҜрқ‘Ҷtopplus-or-minustrрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ңitalic-Пөsubscriptnormрқ‘Ӣрқҗ№subscriptnormрқ‘Ңрқҗ№\operatorname{tr}(({\bar{S}}XD{\bar{S}}^{\top})({\bar{S}}YD{\bar{S}}^{\top}))=\operatorname{tr}(XY)\pm\epsilon\|X\|\_{F}\|Y\|\_{F} with failure probabilityВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.

Note that trвҒЎ(XвҖӢY)trрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң\operatorname{tr}(XY) is here the Frobenius product of Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY.
We omit the proof; it is isomorphic to the proof of CorollaryВ [5](#Thmtheorem5 "Corollary 5. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

To prove TheoremВ [15](#Thmtheorem15 "Theorem 15. вҖЈ 2.3 Hopfield Nets and HopfieldВұ вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we will use the Hanson-Wright inequality.
In its statement,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | вҲҘXвҲҘПҲ2=inf{KвҲЈрқ”ј(exp(X2/K2)вүӨ2}\|X\|\_{\psi\_{2}}=\inf\{K\mid{\mathbb{E}}(\exp(X^{2}/K^{2})\leq 2\} |  |

is the sub-Gaussian norm of random variable Xрқ‘ӢX, which in our case, for a Rademacher variable, will be 1/logвҒЎ2121/\sqrt{\log 2}.

##### Theorem 38 (Hanson-Wright inequality, [rudelson\_hanson-wright\_2013]).

Let xвҲҲв„қdрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptв„қрқ‘‘x\in\mathbb{R}^{d} be a random vector with independent entries,

Let AрқҗҙA be an nГ—nрқ‘ӣрқ‘ӣn\times n matrix.
Then for every tвүҘ0рқ‘Ў0t\geq 0,

where c is some positive constant.

The simplifications also use the fact that Vрқ‘үV and Dрқҗ·D commute and D2superscriptрқҗ·2D^{2} is a projection matrix.

We will apply the Hanson-Wright inequality, for which we need to bound вҖ–VвҖӢ(EвҲҳE)вҖӢVвҖ–F2superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘үрқҗёрқҗёрқ‘үрқҗ№2\|V(E\circ E)V\|\_{F}^{2}.
First, we bound the entries of EрқҗёE: each such entry is 1m1рқ‘ҡ\frac{1}{m} times a sum of mрқ‘ҡm independent Rademacher values, and therefore from TheoremВ [29](#Thmtheorem29 "Theorem 29. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") is at most 1mвҖӢ2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ1)1рқ‘ҡ22subscriptрқӣҝ1\frac{1}{\sqrt{m}}\sqrt{2\log(2/\delta\_{1})} with failure probability Оҙ1subscriptрқӣҝ1\delta\_{1}.
By applying a union bound to all dвҖӢ(dвҲ’1)рқ‘‘рқ‘‘1d(d-1) off-diagonal entries of EрқҗёE, we have that all such entries are at most 2mвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ1)2рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘subscriptрқӣҝ1\frac{2}{\sqrt{m}}\sqrt{\log(2d/\delta\_{1})} with failure probabilityВ Оҙ1subscriptрқӣҝ1\delta\_{1}.
Assuming this event, the square of each entry is at most 4mвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ1)4рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘subscriptрқӣҝ1\frac{4}{m}\log(2d/\delta\_{1}).
We have

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | вҖ–VвҖӢ(EвҲҳE)вҖӢVвҖ–F2=вҲ‘i,jвҲҲ[d]ViвҖӢi2вҖӢVjвҖӢj2вҖӢEiвҖӢj4вүӨ16log(2d/Оҙ1)2m2вҖӢвҲ‘i,jвҲҲ[d]ViвҖӢi2вҖӢVjвҖӢj2=16log(2d/Оҙ1)2m2вӢ…вҖ–VвҖ–F4.\|V(E\circ E)V\|\_{F}^{2}=\sum\_{i,j\in[d]}V\_{ii}^{2}V\_{jj}^{2}E\_{ij}^{4}\leq\frac{16\log(2d/\delta\_{1})^{2}}{m^{2}}\sum\_{i,j\in[d]}V\_{ii}^{2}V\_{jj}^{2}=\frac{16\log(2d/\delta\_{1})^{2}}{m^{2}}\cdot\|V\|\_{F}^{4}. |  |

We will apply TheoremВ [38](#Thmtheorem38 "Theorem 38 (Hanson-Wright inequality, [rudelson_hanson-wright_2013]). вҖЈ 5.2 HopfieldВұ: Autocorrelation Associative Memories as VSAs вҖЈ 5 Autocorrelation Associative Memories as Bundles of Robust Bindings вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") with xрқ‘Ҙx and AрқҗҙA of the theorem mapping to bрқ‘Ҹb and VвҖӢ(EвҲҳE)вҖӢVрқ‘үрқҗёрқҗёрқ‘үV(E\circ E)V.

subscriptрқ”јрқ‘Ҹdelimited-[]subscriptрқ‘Ҹрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҹрқ‘—вҖҰрқ‘–

The value of tрқ‘Ўt in the last line of TheoremВ [38](#Thmtheorem38 "Theorem 38 (Hanson-Wright inequality, [rudelson_hanson-wright_2013]). вҖЈ 5.2 HopfieldВұ: Autocorrelation Associative Memories as VSAs вҖЈ 5 Autocorrelation Associative Memories as Bundles of Robust Bindings вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") translates here to

|  |  |  |

|  | bвҠӨвҖӢVвҖӢ(EвҲҳE)вҖӢVвҖӢbвүӨclogвҒЎ(2)вӢ…4вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ1)mвӢ…вҖ–VвҖ–F2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ2)superscriptрқ‘Ҹtopрқ‘үрқҗёрқҗёрқ‘үрқ‘ҸвӢ…рқ‘җ242рқ‘‘subscriptрқӣҝ1рқ‘ҡsuperscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘үрқҗ№21subscriptрқӣҝ2b^{\top}V(E\circ E)Vb\leq\frac{c}{\log(2)}\cdot\frac{4\log(2d/\delta\_{1})}{m}\cdot\|V\|\_{F}^{2}\log(1/\delta\_{2}) |  |

with failure probability Оҙ2subscriptрқӣҝ2\delta\_{2}, using вҖ–XвҖ–ПҲ2=1/2subscriptnormрқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқң“212\|X\|\_{\psi\_{2}}=1/\sqrt{2}, for XвҲј{Вұ1}similar-toрқ‘Ӣplus-or-minus1X\sim\{\pm 1\}.

### 6 Analysis of MAP-B

We will analyze membership testing for MAP-B, for bundles (В§[6.1](#S6.SS1 "6.1 Bundling вҖЈ 6 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), sequences of sets as encoded with rotations (В§[6.2](#S6.SS2 "6.2 Rotations вҖЈ 6 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), and bundles of bound key-value pairs (В§[6.3](#S6.SS3 "6.3 Binding вҖЈ 6 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")). Here being a key-value pair means that some restrictions are placed on members of a bound pair, in particular that the keys come from a set that is disjoint from the set of values, and so there is greater independence among the relevant random variables.

Recall that the MAP-B bundling operator is signвҒЎ(SвҖӢv)signрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ј\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sv), where Sрқ‘ҶS is a sign matrix, Def.В [2](#Thmtheorem2 "Definition 2. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"),
and the sign function takes a random Вұ1plus-or-minus1\pm 1 value when its argument is zero.

#### 6.1 Bundling

##### 6.1.1 Membership Test

We first consider testing membership in a MAP-B bundling of nрқ‘ӣn atomic vectors.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

For vвҲҲ{0,1}dрқ‘Јsuperscript01рқ‘‘v\in\{0,1\}^{d},
let x=signвҒЎ(SвҖӢv)рқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Јx=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sv) be the MAP-B bundling of n=вҖ–vвҖ–1рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1n=\|v\|\_{1} atomic vectors.
Then for all iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m] and jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v), PrвҒЎ[xiвҖӢSiвҖӢj=+1]=1/2+ОҳвҖӢ(1/n)Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘–рқ‘—112Оҳ1рқ‘ӣ\Pr[x\_{i}S\_{ij}=+1]=1/2+\Theta(1/\sqrt{n}), as nвҶ’вҲһвҶ’рқ‘ӣn\rightarrow\infty, and there is m=OвҖӢ(nвҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ӣрқ‘‘рқӣҝm=O(n\log(d/\delta)) such that with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta,
jвҲҲ[d]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘‘j\in[d] has jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v) if and only if xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j=ejвҠӨвҖӢSвҖӢsignвҒЎ(SвҖӢv)superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—superscriptsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—topрқ‘Ҷsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Јx^{\top}S\_{\*j}=e\_{j}^{\top}S\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sv) has xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—jвүҘ2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ)superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—2рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘рқӣҝx^{\top}S\_{\*j}\geq\sqrt{2m\log(2d/\delta)}.

Note that MAP-B bundling is not associative, so analysis of this bundling operation is not the end of the story, as discussed in В§[6.1.2](#S6.SS1.SSS2 "6.1.2 Dependence on Depth вҖЈ 6.1 Bundling вҖЈ 6 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

##### Proof.

We consider SвҲ—jвҠӨвҖӢxsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—topрқ‘ҘS\_{\*j}^{\top}x in the two cases where jрқ‘—j is, and is not, in suppвҒЎ(v)suppрқ‘Ј\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v).
Fix some j^вҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)^рқ‘—suppрқ‘Ј\hat{j}\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v), and let a=S1вҖӢj^рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ1^рқ‘—a=S\_{1\hat{j}} and b=(SвҖӢv)1вҲ’aрқ‘Ҹsubscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ј1рқ‘Һb=(Sv)\_{1}-a, so that x1=signвҒЎ(a+b)subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1signрқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹx\_{1}=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(a+b), and aвҖӢsignвҒЎ((a+b))=signвҒЎ(aвҖӢ(a+b))рқ‘Һsignрқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹsignрқ‘Һрқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹa\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}((a+b))=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(a(a+b)) is a summand of SвҲ—j^вҠӨвҖӢxsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsent^рқ‘—topрқ‘ҘS\_{\*\hat{j}}^{\top}x.
We consider the cases where nвҲ’1рқ‘ӣ1n-1 is even vs. odd. Let в„°в„°{\mathcal{E}} denote the event signвҒЎ(aвҖӢ(a+b))>0signрқ‘Һрқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹ0\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(a(a+b))>0.

Since the nвҲ’1рқ‘ӣ1n-1 summands of b=(SвҖӢv)1вҲ’aрқ‘Ҹsubscriptрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Ј1рқ‘Һb=(Sv)\_{1}-a are i.i.d. Rademacher variables, the probability that b=0рқ‘Ҹ0b=0 is, for nвҲ’1рқ‘ӣ1n-1 even, equal to
(2вҖӢpp)вҖӢ122вҖӢp=1ПҖвҖӢpвҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/p))=2ПҖвҖӢnвҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/n))binomial2рқ‘қрқ‘қ1superscript22рқ‘қ1рқңӢрқ‘қ1рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘қ2рқңӢрқ‘ӣ1рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘ӣ\binom{2p}{p}\frac{1}{2^{2p}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{\pi p}}(1+O(1/p))=\sqrt{\frac{2}{\pi n}}(1+O(1/n)),
where p=(nвҲ’1)/2рқ‘қрқ‘ӣ12p=(n-1)/2, using StirlingвҖҷs approximation, or the related expression for the Catalan numbers.
For nвҲ’1рқ‘ӣ1n-1 even, when bвү 0рқ‘Ҹ0b\neq 0, |b|>=2рқ‘Ҹ2|b|>=2, so a+b>0рқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹ0a+b>0, and PrвҒЎ[в„°|bвү 0]=1/2Prconditionalв„°рқ‘Ҹ012\Pr[{\mathcal{E}}|b\neq 0]=1/2. We have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[в„°]Prв„°\displaystyle\Pr[{\mathcal{E}}] | =PrвҒЎ[в„°вҲЈb=0]вҖӢPrвҒЎ[b=0]+PrвҒЎ[в„°вҲЈbвү 0]вҖӢPrвҒЎ[bвү 0]absentPrconditionalв„°рқ‘Ҹ0Prрқ‘Ҹ0Prconditionalв„°рқ‘Ҹ0Prрқ‘Ҹ0\displaystyle=\Pr[{\mathcal{E}}\mid b=0]\Pr[b=0]+\Pr[{\mathcal{E}}\mid b\neq 0]\Pr[b\neq 0] |  |

|  |  | =PrвҒЎ[b=0]+12вҖӢ(1вҲ’PrвҒЎ[b=0])absentPrрқ‘Ҹ0121Prрқ‘Ҹ0\displaystyle=\Pr[b=0]+\frac{1}{2}(1-\Pr[b=0]) |  |
|  |  |  |  |

When nвҲ’1рқ‘ӣ1n-1 is odd, bрқ‘Ҹb cannot be zero, while

|  |  |  |

Considering the rounding for the case a+b=0рқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹ0a+b=0, we have
PrвҒЎ[в„°вҲЈb=Вұ1]=3/2Prconditionalв„°рқ‘Ҹplus-or-minus132\Pr[{\mathcal{E}}\mid b=\pm 1]=3/2. Therefore,

So

This applies to all coordinates of all vectors Si,jsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘–рқ‘—S\_{i,j} for jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v), and inspection of the expressions shows the first claim of the theorem,

рқ‘–рқ‘—i,j.

For the remaining claim: we have that xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—jsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—x^{\top}S\_{\*j} for jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v) is a sum of Вұ1plus-or-minus1\pm 1 independent values, with +11+1 having probability 1/2+ОҳвҖӢ(1/n)12Оҳ1рқ‘ӣ1/2+\Theta(1/\sqrt{n}), and at least 1/2+1/7вҖӢn1217рқ‘ӣ1/2+\sqrt{1/7n}, for large enough nрқ‘ӣn; this implies expectation at least m/7вҖӢnрқ‘ҡ7рқ‘ӣm/\sqrt{7n}.
HoeffdingвҖҷs inequality implies that

|  |  |  |

|  | PrвҒЎ[xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j>2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ)]вүӨОҙ/2вҖӢd.Prsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—2рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘рқӣҝрқӣҝ2рқ‘‘\Pr[x^{\top}S\_{\*j}>\sqrt{2m\log(2d/\delta)}]\leq\delta/2d. |  |

Thus, there is m=OвҖӢ(nвҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ӣрқ‘‘рқӣҝm=O(n\log(d/\delta)) such that m/7вҖӢn>2вҖӢ2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ)рқ‘ҡ7рқ‘ӣ22рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘рқӣҝm/\sqrt{7n}>2\sqrt{2m\log(2d/\delta)}, and therefore by a union bound for all jвҲҲ[d]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘‘j\in[d], with failure probability at most Оҙрқӣҝ\delta,
xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j>2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2вҖӢd/Оҙ)superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptрқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—2рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘‘рқӣҝx^{\top}S\_{\*j}>\sqrt{2m\log(2d/\delta)} if an only if jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v).

##### 6.1.2 Dependence on Depth

Instead of bundling a set of elements all at once, suppose instead that bundling is done as a sequence of operations. We will see that for some such sequences, with high depth, so much information is lost that accurate membership tests become impossible.

##### Lemma (Restatement of Lemma [17](#Thmtheorem17 "Lemma 17. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Given independent sign vectors x(i)вҲҲ{Вұ1}m,iвҲҲ[r]formulae-sequencesuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҹx^{(i)}\in\{\pm 1\}^{m},i\in[r], construct vectorВ xрқ‘Ҙx by setting xвҶҗx(1)вҶҗрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x\leftarrow x^{(1)}, and for j=2,вҖҰ,rрқ‘—

2вҖҰрқ‘ҹj=2,\ldots,r, setting xвҶҗsignвҒЎ(x+x(j))вҶҗрқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—x\leftarrow\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(x+x^{(j)}).
Then, for в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m],

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[xв„“(1)вҖӢxв„“=1]=1/2+1/2rPrsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1в„“subscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“1121superscript2рқ‘ҹ\Pr[x^{(1)}\_{\ell}x\_{\ell}=1]=1/2+1/2^{r} |  |

##### Proof.

We consider x1(1)вҖӢx1subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ11subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)}\_{1}x\_{1}; the same analysis applies to xв„“(1)вҖӢxв„“subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1в„“subscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“x^{(1)}\_{\ell}x\_{\ell} for в„“>1в„“1\ell>1.
Let aрқ‘Һa denote x1(1)subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ11x^{(1)}\_{1}, and let z(j)subscriptрқ‘§рқ‘—z\_{(j)} denote the value of x1subscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x\_{1} just after the assignment xвҶҗsignвҒЎ(x+x(j))вҶҗрқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—x\leftarrow\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(x+x^{(j)}) in computingВ xрқ‘Ҙx.
Since bвҖӢsignвҒЎ(c+e)=signвҒЎ(bвҖӢc+bвҖӢe)рқ‘Ҹsignрқ‘җрқ‘’signрқ‘Ҹрқ‘җрқ‘Ҹрқ‘’b\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(c+e)=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(bc+be) for b=Вұ1рқ‘Ҹplus-or-minus1b=\pm 1, we have that

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | x1x1(1)=az(r)=sign(az(rвҲ’1))+ax(r)).x\_{1}x^{(1)}\_{1}=az\_{(r)}=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(az\_{(r-1)})+ax^{(r)}). |  |

By induction on jрқ‘—j with this base case,
az(rвҲ’j))=sign(az(rвҲ’(j+1)))+ax(rвҲ’j))az\_{(r-j)})=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(az\_{(r-(j+1))})+ax^{(r-j)}), ending with aвҖӢz(1)=a2=1рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘§1superscriptрқ‘Һ21az\_{(1)}=a^{2}=1.
Suppose inductively on jрқ‘—j (in the other direction) that aвҖӢz(j)рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘§рқ‘—az\_{(j)} is +11+1 with probability 1/2+1/2j121superscript2рқ‘—1/2+1/2^{j}, respectively; this is true for j=1рқ‘—1j=1, as noted.
We have
az(j)=sign(az(jвҲ’1))+ax(j))az\_{(j)}=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(az\_{(j-1)})+ax^{(j)}), and aвҖӢx(j)=Вұ1рқ‘Һsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘—plus-or-minus1ax^{(j)}=\pm 1 with equal probability independent of aвҖӢz(jвҲ’1)рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘§рқ‘—1az\_{(j-1)}.
Analysis of the four combinations az(jвҲ’1))=Вұ1,ax(j)=Вұ1az\_{(j-1)})=\pm 1,ax^{(j)}=\pm 1 and their probabilities shows that the inductive step holds, that is, aвҖӢz(j+1)рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘§рқ‘—1az\_{(j+1)} is +11+1 with probability 1/2+1/2j+1121superscript2рқ‘—11/2+1/2^{j+1}.
In particular,
PrвҒЎ[x1вҖӢx1(1)=aвҖӢz(r)=+1]=1/2+1/2rPrsubscriptрқ‘Ҙ1subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ11рқ‘Һsubscriptрқ‘§рқ‘ҹ1121superscript2рқ‘ҹ\Pr[x\_{1}x^{(1)}\_{1}=az\_{(r)}=+1]=1/2+1/2^{r}, as claimed.
вҲҺ

Note that this property of xв„“вҖӢxв„“(1)subscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1в„“x\_{\ell}x^{(1)}\_{\ell} does not require the x(i)superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x^{(i)} to be atomic vectors of theВ VSA.
Considering such summands for xвҠӨвҖӢx(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{\top}x^{(1)} leads to
рқ”јвҖӢ[xвҠӨвҖӢx(1)]вүҲm/2rрқ”јdelimited-[]superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1рқ‘ҡsuperscript2рқ‘ҹ{\mathbb{E}}[x^{\top}x^{(1)}]\approx m/2^{r}, as compared to at least m/7вҖӢnрқ‘ҡ7рқ‘ӣm/\sqrt{7n} as in TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), with a corresponding change in mрқ‘ҡm needed to obtain effective membership testing.
Suppose all the x(i)superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x^{(i)} are bundles, and xрқ‘Ҙx is the root of a tree of bundlings of a total ofВ nрқ‘ӣn vectors.
Then x(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)} is a leaf of a tree of bundling operations of depth at leastВ rрқ‘ҹr, with possibly n=rрқ‘ӣрқ‘ҹn=r, when all x(i)superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x^{(i)} involved with x(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)} are atomic; n=2rрқ‘ӣsuperscript2рқ‘ҹn=2^{r}, when xрқ‘Ҙx is the root of a complete binary tree of depth rрқ‘ҹr; or n>2rрқ‘ӣsuperscript2рқ‘ҹn>2^{r}, when x(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)} is not at the maximum depth, or when a single bundling operation involves more than two vectors.
Thus for membership testing to be effective, mрқ‘ҡmВ might need to be at large as 4nsuperscript4рқ‘ӣ4^{n}, or as small asВ O~вҖӢ(n)~рқ‘Ӯрқ‘ӣ\tilde{O}(n), depending on operation depth in computing xрқ‘Ҙx.

The following lemma puts x(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)} in a more general bundle.

##### Corollary 39.

Given independent sign vectors x(i)вҲҲ{Вұ1}msuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡx^{(i)}\in\{\pm 1\}^{m} for iвҲҲ[nвҖІ]рқ‘–delimited-[]superscriptрқ‘ӣвҖІi\in[n^{\prime}] and y(j)вҲҲ{Вұ1}msuperscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘—superscriptplus-or-minus1рқ‘ҡy^{(j)}\in\{\pm 1\}^{m} for jвҲҲ[r]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘ҹj\in[r], construct vectorВ xрқ‘Ҙx by setting xвҶҗsignвҒЎ(вҲ‘iвҲҲnвҖІx(i))вҶҗрқ‘Ҙsignsubscriptрқ‘–superscriptрқ‘ӣвҖІsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–x\leftarrow\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(\sum\_{i\in n^{\prime}}x^{(i)}), and then
for j=1,вҖҰ,rрқ‘—

1вҖҰрқ‘ҹj=1,\ldots,r, setting xвҶҗsignвҒЎ(x+y(j))вҶҗрқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘—x\leftarrow\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(x+y^{(j)}).
Then, for в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m],

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[xв„“(1)вҖӢxв„“=1]=12+12rвҖӢОҳвҖӢ(1n)Prsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1в„“subscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“1121superscript2рқ‘ҹОҳ1рқ‘ӣ\Pr[x^{(1)}\_{\ell}x\_{\ell}=1]=\frac{1}{2}+\frac{1}{2^{r}}\Theta\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{n}}\right) |  |

##### Proof.

Combine the analysis of TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") with the lemma just above.

вҲҺ

Note that this corollary covers any sequence of operations yielding a vector of the form x(1)вҠ•ydirect-sumsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙ1рқ‘Ұx^{(1)}\oplus y, that is x(1)superscriptрқ‘Ҙ1x^{(1)} bundled with yрқ‘Ұy, regardless of how yрқ‘Ұy was computed in the MAP-B algebra.

##### 6.1.3 Testing for Empty Intersection

In this section, rather than estimating set intersection size, we aim for bounds on mрқ‘ҡm so that we can distinguish between nonempty and empty set intersections.
Estimating the set intersection *size* will depend on a rather complicated convolution of Rademacher random variable; the question of distinguishing emptiness has a much cleaner analysis.

Throughout this section, we assume that the elements comprising Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY were all bundled during the same operation.
In other words, they correspond to a depth-1 bundling tree, in the language of the previous section.

##### Lemma 40.

Let X,YвҠҶ[d]

рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң
delimited-[]рқ‘‘X,Y\subseteq[d], and use xрқ‘Ҙx and yрқ‘Ұy to denote their respective MAP-B vectors.
If we choose dimension mвүҘО©вҖӢ(logвҒЎ(1/Оҙ)вӢ…|X|вҖӢ|Y|)рқ‘ҡО©вӢ…1рқӣҝрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ңm\geq\Omega\left(\log(1/\delta)\cdot|X||Y|\right), we can distinguish between the cases |XвҲ©Y|=0рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң0|X\cap Y|=0 and |XвҲ©Y|вүҘ1рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң1|X\cap Y|\geq 1, using the criterion of whether xTвҖӢysuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Үрқ‘Ұx^{T}y is smaller or greater than 2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)2рқ‘ҡ2рқӣҝ\sqrt{2m\log(2/\delta)}.

##### Proof.

Let v,wвҲҲ{0,1}d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscript01рқ‘‘v,w\in\{0,1\}^{d} be characteristic vectors for the sets X,YвҠҶ[d]

рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң
delimited-[]рқ‘‘X,Y\subseteq[d].
First, if |XвҲ©Y|=0рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң0|X\cap Y|=0, their MAP-B bundles x=signвҒЎ(SвҖӢv)рқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Јx=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sv) and y=signвҒЎ(SвҖӢw)рқ‘Ұsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Өy=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sw) are independent, and for any coordinate в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m]:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“]=PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=1]вҲ’PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=вҲ’1]=0рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“10{\mathbb{E}}[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}]=\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=1]-\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=-1]=0 |  |

Using Theorem [29](#Thmtheorem29 "Theorem 29. вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we conclude that with probability 1вҲ’Оҙ21рқӣҝ21-\frac{\delta}{2}, we satisfy xвҠӨвҖӢyвүӨ2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)вӢ…msuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopрқ‘ҰвӢ…22рқӣҝрқ‘ҡx^{\top}y\leq\sqrt{2\log(2/\delta)\cdot m}.

Now, suppose |XвҲ©Y|=1рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң1|X\cap Y|=1.
Then, we can use eвҲ—superscriptрқ‘’e^{\*} to denote the standard basis vector that represents the element in their intersection.
Let x=signвҒЎ(SвҖӢv)рқ‘Ҙsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Јx=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sv) and y=signвҒЎ(SвҖӢw)рқ‘Ұsignрқ‘Ҷрқ‘Өy=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(Sw) be the MAP-B bundles representing Xрқ‘ӢX and Yрқ‘ҢY.
(Here, Sрқ‘ҶS is a random sign matrix; see Definition [2](#Thmtheorem2 "Definition 2. вҖЈ Bundling and Set Intersection вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").)

Since all coordinates within xрқ‘Ҙx are independent of each other (and likewise for yрқ‘Ұy), it suffices to understand the distribution of a single coordinate.
Fix в„“вҲҲ[m]в„“delimited-[]рқ‘ҡ\ell\in[m]. We will study the quantities PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=1]Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=1] and PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=вҲ’1]Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=-1] to eventually obtain a concentration bound for xвҠӨвҖӢysuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopрқ‘Ұx^{\top}y.

Let Z(X)=(SвҖӢeвҲ—)в„“+вҲ‘iвҲҲXвҲ–YZi(X)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘’в„“subscriptрқ‘–рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ңsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘–рқ‘ӢZ^{(X)}=(Se^{\*})\_{\ell}+\sum\_{i\in X\setminus Y}Z\_{i}^{(X)}, where the {Zi(X)}i=1msuperscriptsubscriptsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘–рқ‘Ӣрқ‘–1рқ‘ҡ\{Z\_{i}^{(X)}\}\_{i=1}^{m} are independent Rademacher variables coming from the в„“в„“\ell-th coordinates of the atomic vectors that were bundled to form Xрқ‘ӢX.
Define Z(Y)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘ҢZ^{(Y)} similarly for Yрқ‘ҢY, and let XвҖІ=Z(X)вҲ’(SвҖӢeвҲ—)в„“superscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІsuperscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘Ӣsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘’в„“X^{\prime}=Z^{(X)}-(Se^{\*})\_{\ell} and YвҖІ=Z(Y)вҲ’(SвҖӢeвҲ—)в„“superscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІsuperscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘Ңsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘’в„“Y^{\prime}=Z^{(Y)}-(Se^{\*})\_{\ell}.

First, assume |XвҲ–Y|рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң|X\setminus Y| and |YвҲ–X|рқ‘Ңрқ‘Ӣ|Y\setminus X| are both even. The other cases follow similarly; the only change to track is that when |XвҲ–Y|рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң|X\setminus Y| (or |YвҲ–X|рқ‘Ңрқ‘Ӣ|Y\setminus X|) is odd, Z(X)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘ӢZ^{(X)} (resp. Z(Y)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘ҢZ^{(Y)}) could be 00, and we have a 1212\frac{1}{2} chance of Z(X)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘ӢZ^{(X)} (resp. Z(Y)superscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘ҢZ^{(Y)}) being positive and a 1212\frac{1}{2} chance it is negative.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[xв„“=yв„“=1]Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1\displaystyle\Pr[x\_{\ell}=y\_{\ell}=1] | =PrвҒЎ[Z(X)=Z(Y)=1]absentPrsuperscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘Ӣsuperscriptрқ‘Қрқ‘Ң1\displaystyle=\Pr[Z^{(X)}=Z^{(Y)}=1] |  |

|  |  | =PrвҒЎ[XвҖІвүҘ0,YвҖІвүҘ0]вӢ…PrвҒЎ[(SвҖӢeвҲ—)в„“=1]+PrвҒЎ[XвҖІвүӨ1,YвҖІвүӨ1]вӢ…PrвҒЎ[(SвҖӢeвҲ—)в„“=вҲ’1]absentвӢ…Prsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІ0superscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІ0Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘’в„“1вӢ…Prsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІ1superscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІ1Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘’в„“1\displaystyle=\Pr[X^{\prime}\geq 0,Y^{\prime}\geq 0]\cdot\Pr[(Se^{\*})\_{\ell}=1]+\Pr[X^{\prime}\leq 1,Y^{\prime}\leq 1]\cdot\Pr[(Se^{\*})\_{\ell}=-1] |  |

Combining these terms, the quantity PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=1]вҲ’PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=вҲ’1]Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=1]-\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=-1] is equal to:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | (PrвҒЎ[XвҖІвүҘ0]вҲ’PrвҒЎ[XвҖІ<0])вӢ…(PrвҒЎ[YвҖІвүҘ0]вҲ’PrвҒЎ[YвҖІ<0])=PrвҒЎ[XвҖІ=0]вӢ…PrвҒЎ[YвҖІ=0]вӢ…Prsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІ0Prsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІ0Prsuperscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІ0Prsuperscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІ0вӢ…Prsuperscriptрқ‘ӢвҖІ0Prsuperscriptрқ‘ҢвҖІ0\displaystyle\left(\Pr[X^{\prime}\geq 0]-\Pr[X^{\prime}<0]\right)\cdot\left(\Pr[Y^{\prime}\geq 0]-\Pr[Y^{\prime}<0]\right)=\Pr[X^{\prime}=0]\cdot\Pr[Y^{\prime}=0] |  | (7) |

Again using the fact that (2вҖӢpp)вҖӢ122вҖӢp=1ПҖвҖӢpвҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/p))=2ПҖвҖӢnвҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/n))binomial2рқ‘қрқ‘қ1superscript22рқ‘қ1рқңӢрқ‘қ1рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘қ2рқңӢрқ‘ӣ1рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘ӣ\binom{2p}{p}\frac{1}{2^{2p}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{\pi p}}(1+O(1/p))=\sqrt{\frac{2}{\pi n}}(1+O(1/n)) (which was also used in the membership test), we have PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=1]вҲ’PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=вҲ’1]вүҘО©вҖӢ(1|X|вӢ…|Y|)Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“1О©1вӢ…рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ң\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=1]-\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=-1]\geq\Omega\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{|X|\cdot|Y|}}\right).

Define pвүЎCвҖІвӢ…1|X|вӢ…|Y|рқ‘қвӢ…superscriptрқҗ¶вҖІ1вӢ…рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ңp\equiv C^{\prime}\cdot\frac{1}{\sqrt{|X|\cdot|Y|}}, so PrвҒЎ[xв„“вҖӢyв„“=1]вүҘ1+p2Prsubscriptрқ‘Ҙв„“subscriptрқ‘Ұв„“11рқ‘қ2\Pr[x\_{\ell}y\_{\ell}=1]\geq\frac{1+p}{2}.
Applying the Chernoff bound for a sum of mрқ‘ҡm Rademachers, we have:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Pr[(xвҠӨyвүҘm2+pвҖӢm2вҲ’2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)вӢ…m]вүҘ1вҲ’Оҙ2\displaystyle\Pr\left[(x^{\top}y\geq\frac{m}{2}+\frac{pm}{2}-\sqrt{2\log(2/\delta)\cdot m}\right]\geq 1-\frac{\delta}{2} |  |

In order to distinguish between the two cases, we require pвҖӢm2вүҘ2вҖӢ2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)вӢ…mрқ‘қрқ‘ҡ22вӢ…22рқӣҝрқ‘ҡ\frac{pm}{2}\geq 2\sqrt{2\log(2/\delta)\cdot m}, so we need to choose mвүҘО©вҖӢ(logвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)p2)рқ‘ҡО©2рқӣҝsuperscriptрқ‘қ2m\geq\Omega\left(\frac{\log(2/\delta)}{p^{2}}\right).
вҲҺ

##### Remark 41.

If we have |X|=nрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ӣ|X|=n and |Y|=1рқ‘Ң1|Y|=1, and enforce a failure probability of Оҙdрқӣҝрқ‘‘\frac{\delta}{d} (so that we can union bound over all atomic vectors that represent [d]delimited-[]рқ‘‘[d]), we recover the result of Lemma [6.1](#S6.SS1 "6.1 Bundling вҖЈ 6 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

#### 6.2 Rotations

Here we consider membership testing, leveraging TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") in a simple way.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [18](#Thmtheorem18 "Theorem 18. вҖЈ Rotations and Bundles of Bindings вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Given a sign matrix SвҲҲIвҖӢRmГ—dрқ‘ҶsuperscriptIRрқ‘ҡрқ‘‘S\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{m\times d} and rotation matrix RвҲҲIвҖӢRmГ—mрқ‘…superscriptIRрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҡR\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{m\times m}, and integer length LрқҗҝL.
Recall (Def.В [8](#Thmtheorem8 "Definition 8. вҖЈ Rotations via JL property. вҖЈ 2.2 Analysis of MAP-I Using Johnson-Lindenstrauss вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) that SR,LвүЎ[SвҖӢRвҖӢSвҖӢR2вҖӢSвҖӢвҖҰвҖӢRLвҲ’1вҖӢS]subscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘…рқҗҝdelimited-[]рқ‘Ҷрқ‘…рқ‘Ҷsuperscriptрқ‘…2рқ‘ҶвҖҰsuperscriptрқ‘…рқҗҝ1рқ‘ҶS\_{R,L}\equiv[S\;RS\;R^{2}S\;\ldots R^{L-1}S].
For a sequence of dрқ‘‘d-vectors v(0),v(1),вҖҰвҖӢv(LвҲ’1)вҲҲ{0,1}d

subscriptрқ‘Ј0subscriptрқ‘Ј1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Јрқҗҝ1
superscript01рқ‘‘v\_{(0)},v\_{(1)},\ldots v\_{(L-1)}\in\{0,1\}^{d},
let vвүЎ[v(0)вҖӢv(1)вҖӢвҖҰвҖӢv(LвҲ’1)]рқ‘Јdelimited-[]subscriptрқ‘Ј0subscriptрқ‘Ј1вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Јрқҗҝ1v\equiv[v\_{(0)}\;v\_{(1)}\;\ldots v\_{(L-1)}], let x=signвҒЎ(SR,LвҖӢv)рқ‘Ҙsignsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘…рқҗҝрқ‘Јx=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(S\_{R,L}v), and let n=вҖ–vвҖ–1рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1n=\|v\|\_{1}.
Then there is m=OвҖӢ(LвҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(LвҖӢd/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқҗҝрқ‘ӣрқҗҝрқ‘‘рқӣҝm=O(Ln\log(Ld/\delta)) such that with failure probability at most Оҙрқӣҝ\delta,
jвҲҲ[LвҖӢd]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқҗҝрқ‘‘j\in[Ld] has jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v) if and only if xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—,j%dвүҘ2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(LвҖӢd/Оҙ)x^{\top}S\_{\*,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}\geq 2\sqrt{m\log(Ld/\delta)},
where j%dвүЎ1+(jвҲ’1)moddj\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}\equiv 1+(j-1)\mod d.

##### Proof.

Consider

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—,j%d=вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]xiвҖӢSi,j%d=вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]Si,j%dвҖӢ(SR,L)i,вҲ—вҖӢv=1+вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]Si,j%dвҖӢ((SR,L)i,вҲ—вҖӢvвҲ’Si,j%d).x^{\top}S\_{\*,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}=\sum\_{i\in[m]}x\_{i}S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}=\sum\_{i\in[m]}S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}(S\_{R,L})\_{i,\*}v=1+\sum\_{i\in[m]}S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}((S\_{R,L})\_{i,\*}v-S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}). |  |

The random variables of Sрқ‘ҶS that appear in Si,j%dвҖӢ((SR,L)i,вҲ—вҖӢvвҲ’Si,j%d)S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}((S\_{R,L})\_{i,\*}v-S\_{i,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}})
cannot appear in

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Si+L,j%dвҖӢ((SR,L)i+L,вҲ—вҖӢvвҲ’Si+L,j%d),S\_{i+L,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}((S\_{R,L})\_{i+L,\*}v-S\_{i+L,j\_{{\scriptscriptstyle\%}d}}), |  |

since the appearances of a given Si,jsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘–рқ‘—S\_{i,j} due to shifting in SR,Lsubscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘…рқҗҝS\_{R,L} only span LрқҗҝL rows.
That is, there are at most LрқҗҝL blocks of at least (m/L)вҲ’1рқ‘ҡрқҗҝ1(m/L)-1 rows such that each block can be analyzed as in TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
We obtain, for a given block of rows, and after taking into account that only (m/L)вҲ’1рқ‘ҡрқҗҝ1(m/L)-1 rows are in a block, that there is m=OвҖӢ(LвҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқҗҝрқ‘ӣрқ‘‘рқӣҝm=O(Ln\log(d/\delta)) such that with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, jвҲҲ[d]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘‘j\in[d] has jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v) if and only if the vectors x~~рқ‘Ҙ\tilde{x} and S~вҲ—jsubscript~рқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—\tilde{S}\_{\*j} corresponding to the block of rows have x~вҠӨвҖӢS~вҲ—jвүҘ2вҖӢ(m/L)вҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ)superscript~рқ‘Ҙtopsubscript~рқ‘Ҷabsentрқ‘—2рқ‘ҡрқҗҝрқ‘‘рқӣҝ\tilde{x}^{\top}\tilde{S}\_{\*j}\geq 2\sqrt{(m/L)\log(d/\delta)}.
By requiring failure probability at most Оҙ/Lрқӣҝрқҗҝ\delta/L, satisfied by m=OвҖӢ(LвҖӢnвҖӢlogвҒЎ(dвҖӢL/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқҗҝрқ‘ӣрқ‘‘рқҗҝрқӣҝm=O(Ln\log(dL/\delta)),
the result follows.
вҲҺ

#### 6.3 Binding

Binding is done in MAP-B the same as in MAP-I, namely, as coordinate-wise product.
Here we also consider membership test in a bundle of bindings, where again we assume that the bundling is done in one step, that is, a sum over the integers followed by the signsign\operatorname{{\text{sign}}} function.

##### 6.3.1 Membership in Key-Value Pairs

We will show the following.

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [20](#Thmtheorem20 "Theorem 20. вҖЈ Rotations and Bundles of Bindings вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Let vвҲҲ{0,1}(d2)рқ‘Јsuperscript01binomialрқ‘‘2v\in\{0,1\}^{\binom{d}{2}} be such that x=signвҒЎ(SвҠҷ2вҖӢv)рқ‘Ҙsignsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Јx=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(S^{\odot 2}v) is a bundle of key-value pairs, as in Def.В [19](#Thmtheorem19 "Definition 19. вҖЈ Rotations and Bundles of Bindings вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
Let n=вҖ–vвҖ–1рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1n=\|v\|\_{1}.
Then there is m=OвҖӢ(nвҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ӣрқ‘‘рқӣҝm=O(n\log(d/\delta)) such that with failure probability at most Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, jвҲҲ[(dk)]рқ‘—delimited-[]binomialрқ‘‘рқ‘ҳj\in[\binom{d}{k}] has jвҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)рқ‘—suppрқ‘Јj\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v) if and only if xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—jвҠҷ2вүҘ2вҖӢmвҖӢlogвҒЎ(d/Оҙ)superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2absentрқ‘—2рқ‘ҡрқ‘‘рқӣҝx^{\top}S^{\odot 2}\_{\*j}\geq 2\sqrt{m\log(d/\delta)}.

The conclusion of the theorem is much the same as that of TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
This is not a coincidence: the analysis of key-value pairs reduces to the same setting as that earlier lemma.

##### Proof.

For jвҲҲ[(d2)]рқ‘—delimited-[]binomialрқ‘‘2j\in[\binom{d}{2}], let wвҖӢ(j)вҲҲW,qвҖӢ(j)вҲҲQformulae-sequenceрқ‘Өрқ‘—рқ‘Ҡрқ‘һрқ‘—рқ‘„w(j)\in W,q(j)\in Q be the indices such that SвҲ—,jвҠҷ2=SвҲ—,wвҖӢ(j)вҲҳSвҲ—,qвҖӢ(j)subscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2

рқ‘—subscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘Өрқ‘—subscriptрқ‘Ҷ

рқ‘һрқ‘—S^{\odot 2}\_{\*,j}=S\_{\*,w(j)}\circ S\_{\*,q(j)}.
Let j^вҲҲsuppвҒЎ(v)^рқ‘—suppрқ‘Ј\hat{j}\in\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v). We have signвҒЎ(xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j^вҠҷ2)=signвҒЎ(1+(SвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҲ’SвҲ—,j^вҠҷ2)вҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—j^вҠҷ2)signsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2absent^рқ‘—sign1superscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Јsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2

^рқ‘—topsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2absent^рқ‘—\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(x^{\top}S^{\odot 2}\_{\*\hat{j}})=\operatorname{{\text{sign}}}(1+(S^{\odot 2}v-S^{\odot 2}\_{\*,\hat{j}})^{\top}S^{\odot 2}\_{\*\hat{j}}), and

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | SвҠҷ2вҖӢvвҲ’SвҲ—,j^вҠҷ2=вҲ‘jвү j^SвҲ—,qвҖӢ(j)вҲҳSвҲ—,wвҖӢ(j).superscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2рқ‘Јsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2  ^рқ‘—subscriptрқ‘—^рқ‘—subscriptрқ‘Ҷ  рқ‘һрқ‘—subscriptрқ‘Ҷ  рқ‘Өрқ‘—S^{\odot 2}v-S^{\odot 2}\_{\*,\hat{j}}=\sum\_{j\neq\hat{j}}S\_{\*,q(j)}\circ S\_{\*,w(j)}. |  |

Since each SвҲ—,qвҖӢ(j)subscriptрқ‘Ҷ

(Whatever the relations among the wвҖӢ(j)рқ‘Өрқ‘—w(j).)
So xвҠӨвҖӢSвҲ—,j^вҠҷ2superscriptрқ‘Ҙtopsubscriptsuperscriptрқ‘Ҷdirect-productabsent2

superscriptрқ‘—вҖІx^{\top}S^{\odot 2}\_{\*,j^{\prime}} for jвҖІвҲүsuppвҒЎ(v)superscriptрқ‘—вҖІsuppрқ‘Јj^{\prime}\notin\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v).
Therefore the same conditions on mрқ‘ҡm imply the same results on failure probability as in TheoremВ [16](#Thmtheorem16 "Theorem 16. вҖЈ 2.4 Analysis of MAP-B вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), and the lemma follows.
вҲҺ

### 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration

We will analyze the VSA dimension needed for reliably estimating the size of the intersection of sets represented by Bloom filters (В§[7.1](#S7.SS1 "7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and Counting Bloom filters (В§[7.2](#S7.SS2 "7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
In the latter, we actually consider a generalization to weighted sets.

#### 7.1 Bloom Filters

In the VSA model described in this section, the atomic vectors are xвҲҲ{0,1}mрқ‘Ҙsuperscript01рқ‘ҡx\in\{0,1\}^{m} where for some kрқ‘ҳk, вҖ–xвҖ–1вүӨksubscriptnormрқ‘Ҙ1рқ‘ҳ\|x\|\_{1}\leq k, with the nonzero entries chosen randomly.
As discussed in Def.В [21](#Thmtheorem21 "Definition 21. вҖЈ 2.5 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), an atomic vector BвҲ—jsubscriptрқҗөabsentрқ‘—B\_{\*j} is created by performing kрқ‘ҳk trials, in each trial picking iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m] uniformly at random and setting BiвҖӢjвҶҗ1вҶҗsubscriptрқҗөрқ‘–рқ‘—1B\_{ij}\leftarrow 1.
(It is possible to pick the same iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m] twice, in which case we only perform the update once.)
Bundling will be done with disjunction, so a set with characteristic vector vвҲҲ{0,1}dрқ‘Јsuperscript01рқ‘‘v\in\{0,1\}^{d} is represented as 1вҲ§BвҖӢv1рқҗөрқ‘Ј1\wedge Bv, meaning that the coordinate-wise minimum of BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv with 1 is taken.

This representation, and the resulting membership testing, has long been studied as used as *Bloom filters*, with many variations, including applications to *private* set intersection estimation.
However, the narrow question of how to use dot products of Bloom filter representations (or other simple vector operations) to estimate set intersection size, is less well developed.
It is outlined briefly in [broder\_network\_2004], and discussed in [swamidass\_mathematical\_2007].
An analysis is given in [papapetrou\_cardinality\_2010], where the assumption is made that the entries of BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv are independent of each other. 222This is a good approximation, but the approximation is not rigorously substantiated, so the results are correct only up to that assumption. See also [bose\_false-positive\_2008] regarding difficulties in the analysis of Bloom filters.
We will bound the error in estimating set intersections using Bloom filters in Theorem [22](#Thmtheorem22 "Theorem 22. вҖЈ 2.5 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

A key quantity for our analysis is the number of nonzeros in BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv as a function of вҖ–vвҖ–0subscriptnormрқ‘Ј0\|v\|\_{0}, when vвҲҲ{0,1}dрқ‘Јsuperscript01рқ‘‘v\in\{0,1\}^{d}.
We will let вҖ–xвҖ–0subscriptnormрқ‘Ҙ0\|x\|\_{0} denote the number of nonzeros of xрқ‘Ҙx, so вҖ–1вҲ§BвҖӢvвҖ–1=вҖ–BвҖӢvвҖ–0subscriptnorm1рқҗөрқ‘Ј1subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ј0\|1\wedge Bv\|\_{1}=\|Bv\|\_{0}.
This includes real numbers yрқ‘Ұy, so вҖ–yвҖ–0subscriptnormрқ‘Ұ0\|y\|\_{0} is one when yвү 0рқ‘Ұ0y\neq 0, and 0 otherwise.

##### Lemma 42.

For vвҲҲ{0,1}dрқ‘Јsuperscript01рқ‘‘v\in\{0,1\}^{d}, let nвүЎвҖ–vвҖ–0рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј0n\equiv\|v\|\_{0}. Define ОәвүЎвҖ–BвҖӢvвҖ–0рқң…subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ј0\kappa\equiv\|Bv\|\_{0}, and let pв„“вүЎ(1вҲ’1/m)kвҖӢв„“subscriptрқ‘қв„“superscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳв„“p\_{\ell}\equiv(1-1/m)^{k\ell}.
Then рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]=mвҖӢ(1вҲ’pn)рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…рқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]=m(1-p\_{n}).
Moreover, letting m~вүЎвҲ’1/logвҒЎ(1вҲ’1/m)~рқ‘ҡ111рқ‘ҡ{\tilde{m}}\equiv-1/\log(1-1/m),

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | 1вҲ’kвҖӢв„“mвҲ’1вүӨpв„“=expвҒЎ(вҲ’kвҖӢв„“/m~)вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’kвҖӢв„“/m)1рқ‘ҳв„“рқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқ‘қв„“рқ‘ҳв„“~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳв„“рқ‘ҡ1-\frac{k\ell}{m-1}\leq p\_{\ell}=\exp(-k\ell/{\tilde{m}})\leq\exp(-k\ell/m) |  | (8) |

Letting hm,kвҖӢ(z)вүЎвҲ’m~kвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’zm)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘§~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘§рқ‘ҡh\_{m,k}(z)\equiv\frac{-{\tilde{m}}}{k}\log(1-\frac{z}{m}), we have hm,kвҖӢ(рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә])=hm,kвҖӢ(mвҖӢ(1вҲ’pn))=nsubscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣрқ‘ӣh\_{m,k}({\mathbb{E}}[\kappa])=h\_{m,k}(m(1-p\_{n}))=n.

Here, we can think of hm,ksubscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳh\_{m,k} as an estimator for вҖ–vвҖ–0subscriptnormрқ‘Ј0\|v\|\_{0}, accounting for collisions in BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv.
It is not unbiased, as we do not have рқ”јвҖӢ[hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)]=nрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…рқ‘ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[h\_{m,k}(\kappa)]=n, but hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…h\_{m,k}(\kappa) will still be a *good* estimator if Оәрқң…\kappa concentrates; luckily for us, it does, as shown below.

The definitions of m~~рқ‘ҡ{\tilde{m}} may also seem a bit curious; we use the following well-known inequalities.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | logвҒЎ(1+x)вүӨxвҖӢforвҖӢallвҖӢxвҲ’logвҒЎ(1вҲ’x)вүӨx1вҲ’xвҖӢforвҖӢx<11рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ҙforallрқ‘Ҙ1рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ҙ1рқ‘Ҙforрқ‘Ҙ1\begin{split}\log(1+x)&\leq x\mathrm{\ for\ all\ }x\\ -\log(1-x)&\leq\frac{x}{1-x}\mathrm{\ for\ }x<1\end{split} |  | (9) |

These imply

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | 1mвүӨвҲ’logвҒЎ(1вҲ’1m)1рқ‘ҡ11рқ‘ҡ\displaystyle\frac{1}{m}\leq-\log(1-\frac{1}{m}) | вүӨ1/m1вҲ’1/m=1mвҲ’1,andвҖӢsoformulae-sequenceabsent1рқ‘ҡ11рқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ҡ1andso\displaystyle\leq\frac{1/m}{1-1/m}=\frac{1}{m-1},\mathrm{\ and\ so} |  | (10) |
|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mвҲ’1вүӨm~рқ‘ҡ1~рқ‘ҡ\displaystyle m-1\leq{\tilde{m}} | вүӨmabsentрқ‘ҡ\displaystyle\leq m |  | (11) |

##### of LemmaВ [42](#Thmtheorem42 "Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

Observe that for each of nрқ‘ӣn vectors BвҲ—jsubscriptрқҗөabsentрқ‘—B\_{\*j}, there will be kрқ‘ҳk independent trials generating random iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m], so for (BвҖӢv)isubscriptрқҗөрқ‘Јрқ‘–(Bv)\_{i} to be zero, all kвҖӢnрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣkn independent trials need to miss indexВ iрқ‘–i.
This happens for a single trial with probability 1вҲ’1/m11рқ‘ҡ1-1/m, and so the probability that all kвҖӢnрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣkn trials miss iрқ‘–i is (1вҲ’1/m)kвҖӢnsuperscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ(1-1/m)^{kn}.
It follows that the expected number of nonzeros

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]=рқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–BвҖӢvвҖ–0]=рқ”јвҖӢ[вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]вҖ–BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvвҖ–0]=вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]рқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvвҖ–0]=mвҖӢ(1вҲ’(1вҲ’1/m)kвҖӢn)=mвҖӢ(1вҲ’pn),рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ј0рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡsubscriptnormsubscriptрқҗө  рқ‘–рқ‘Ј0subscriptрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptnormsubscriptрқҗө  рқ‘–рқ‘Ј0рқ‘ҡ1superscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣрқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]={\mathbb{E}}[\|Bv\|\_{0}]={\mathbb{E}}[\sum\_{i\in[m]}\|B\_{i\*}v\|\_{0}]=\sum\_{i\in[m]}{\mathbb{E}}[\|B\_{i\*}v\|\_{0}]=m(1-(1-1/m)^{kn})=m(1-p\_{n}), |  |

as claimed.
To show ([8](#S7.E8 "In Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), we use ([9](#S7.E9 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and ([10](#S7.E10 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), which imply

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | 1вҲ’kвҖӢв„“mвҲ’1вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’kвҖӢв„“/(mвҲ’1))вүӨ(1вҲ’1m)kвҖӢв„“=pв„“вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’kвҖӢв„“/m),1рқ‘ҳв„“рқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ҳв„“рқ‘ҡ1superscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳв„“subscriptрқ‘қв„“рқ‘ҳв„“рқ‘ҡ1-\frac{k\ell}{m-1}\leq\exp(-k\ell/(m-1))\leq\left(1-\frac{1}{m}\right)^{k\ell}=p\_{\ell}\leq\exp(-k\ell/m), |  |

as claimed. The last claim is immediate.
