##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [22](#Thmtheorem22 "Theorem 22. вҖЈ 2.5 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Let v,wвҲҲ{0,1}d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscript01рқ‘‘v,w\in\{0,1\}^{d} represent sets X,Y

рқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҢX,Y respectively, and define the following counts:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | nвүЎ|XвҲ©Y|=vвӢ…w,nvвүЎ|XвҲ–Y|=вҖ–vвҖ–0вҲ’n,nwвүЎ|YвҲ–X|=вҖ–wвҖ–0вҲ’nformulae-sequenceрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҢвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘Өsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ңsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј0рқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘Ңрқ‘Ӣsubscriptnormрқ‘Ө0рқ‘ӣn\equiv|X\cap Y|=v\cdot w,\;\;\;\;\;\;n\_{v}\equiv|X\setminus Y|=\|v\|\_{0}-n,\;\;\;\;\;\;n\_{w}\equiv|Y\setminus X|=\|w\|\_{0}-n |  |

Let x=1вҲ§BвҖӢvрқ‘Ҙ1рқҗөрқ‘Јx=1\wedge Bv and y=1вҲ§BвҖӢwрқ‘Ұ1рқҗөрқ‘Өy=1\wedge Bw, where BвҲҲ{0,1}mГ—dрқҗөsuperscript01рқ‘ҡрқ‘‘B\in\{0,1\}^{m\times d} is a sparse binary matrix.

Assume WLOG nwвүҘnvsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јn\_{w}\geq n\_{v}.
Then for ОҙвҲҲ(0,1)рқӣҝ01\delta\in(0,1) and Оө>0рқңҖ0{\varepsilon}>0, there are k=OвҖӢ(ОөвҲ’1вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҳрқ‘ӮsuperscriptрқңҖ11рқӣҝk=O({\varepsilon}^{-1}\log(1/\delta))
and m=OвҖӢ(kвҖӢОөвҲ’1вҖӢ(nvвҖӢnw+n2+ОөвҖӢ(n+nw)))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқңҖ1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқңҖрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өm=O(k{\varepsilon}^{-1}(n\_{v}n\_{w}+n^{2}+{\varepsilon}(n+n\_{w}))) such that hm,kвҖӢ(xвӢ…y)=nВұПөsubscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұplus-or-minusрқ‘ӣitalic-Пөh\_{m,k}(x\cdot y)=n\pm\epsilon with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta. Here, hm,kвҖӢ(z)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘§h\_{m,k}(z) (see LemmaВ [42](#Thmtheorem42 "Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) maps the Bloom filter output 1вҲ§BвҖӢz1рқҗөрқ‘§1\wedge Bz to an estimate of вҖ–zвҖ–0subscriptnormрқ‘§0\|z\|\_{0}.

When Оө<1/2рқңҖ12{\varepsilon}<1/2, the integrality of nрқ‘ӣn implies an exact result.
Thus, the theorem implies that when nрқ‘ӣn and nvsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јn\_{v} are OвҖӢ(1)рқ‘Ӯ1O(1), m=OвҖӢ(kвҖӢnw)рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өm=O(kn\_{w}) and k=OвҖӢ(logвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҳрқ‘Ӯ1рқӣҝk=O(\log(1/\delta)) suffice.
This includes the case of membership testing, where nv=1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ј1n\_{v}=1.

The theorem also allows Оө>1рқңҖ1{\varepsilon}>1, including Оө=Оө~вҖӢnрқңҖ~рқңҖрқ‘ӣ{\varepsilon}={\tilde{\varepsilon}}n, which allows us to estimate nрқ‘ӣn up to relative error ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon} rather than additive error ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon}.
In this case, m=OвҖӢ(kвҖӢОө~вҲ’1вҖӢ(nvвҖӢnw/n+n)+kвҖӢnw)рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯрқ‘ҳsuperscript~рқңҖ1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ӣрқ‘ӣрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өm=O(k{\tilde{\varepsilon}}^{-1}(n\_{v}n\_{w}/n+n)+kn\_{w}) and k=OвҖӢ(maxвҒЎ{1,Оө~вҲ’1вҖӢnвҲ’1вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ)})рқ‘ҳрқ‘Ӯ1superscript~рқңҖ1superscriptрқ‘ӣ11рқӣҝk=O(\max\{1,{\tilde{\varepsilon}}^{-1}n^{-1}\log(1/\delta)\}) suffice.

##### Proof.

Let vc=vвҲҳwsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җрқ‘Јрқ‘Өv^{c}=v\circ w, where вҲҳ\circ denotes element-wise product, so n=вҖ–vcвҖ–0рқ‘ӣsubscriptnormsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ0n=\|v^{c}\|\_{0}, and let

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ОәвҲ©=вҖ–BвҖӢvcвҖ–0.subscriptрқң…subscriptnormрқҗөsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ0\kappa\_{\cap}=\|Bv^{c}\|\_{0}. |  |

Let xc=1вҲ§BвҖӢvcsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ1рқҗөsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җx^{c}=1\wedge Bv^{c}, x~=xвҲ’xc~рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ{\tilde{x}}=x-x^{c}, y~=yвҲ’xc~рқ‘Ұрқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ{\tilde{y}}=y-x^{c}, and let

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | ОәО”вүЎx~вӢ…y~=xвӢ…yвҲ’ОәвҲ©,subscriptрқң…О”вӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘ҰвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұsubscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\Delta}\equiv{\tilde{x}}\cdot{\tilde{y}}=x\cdot y-\kappa\_{\cap}, |  |

noting that x~вӢ…xc=0вӢ…~рқ‘Ҙsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ0{\tilde{x}}\cdot x^{c}=0 and y~вӢ…xc=0вӢ…~рқ‘Ұsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ0{\tilde{y}}\cdot x^{c}=0,

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | x~вӢ…y~вӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘Ұ\displaystyle{\tilde{x}}\cdot{\tilde{y}} | =xвӢ…yвҲ’xcвӢ…xвҲ’xcвӢ…y+xcвӢ…xcabsentвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җрқ‘ҘвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җрқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ\displaystyle=x\cdot y-x^{c}\cdot x-x^{c}\cdot y+x^{c}\cdot x^{c} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =xвӢ…yвҲ’(xcвӢ…x~+xcвӢ…xc)вҲ’(xcвӢ…y~+xcвӢ…xc)+xcвӢ…xcabsentвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ~рқ‘ҘвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ~рқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ\displaystyle=x\cdot y-(x^{c}\cdot{\tilde{x}}+x^{c}\cdot x^{c})-(x^{c}\cdot{\tilde{y}}+x^{c}\cdot x^{c})+x^{c}\cdot x^{c} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =xвӢ…yвҲ’xcвӢ…xcabsentвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җsuperscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘җ\displaystyle=x\cdot y-x^{c}\cdot x^{c} |  |

In other words, we can rewrite xвӢ…y=ОәвүЎОәвҲ©+ОәО”вӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұрқң…subscriptрқң…subscriptрқң…О”x\cdot y=\kappa\equiv\kappa\_{\cap}+\kappa\_{\Delta}, where ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} counts the 1s that xрқ‘Ҙx and yрқ‘Ұy have in common due to elements in suppвҒЎ(v)вҲ©suppвҒЎ(w)suppрқ‘Јsuppрқ‘Ө\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v)\cap\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(w), while ОәО”subscriptрқң…О”\kappa\_{\Delta} counts the 1s common to x,y

рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұx,y due to elements corresponding to the symmetric difference suppвҒЎ(|vвҲ’w|)=suppвҒЎ(v)вҖӢО”вҖӢsuppвҒЎ(w)suppрқ‘Јрқ‘Өsuppрқ‘ЈО”suppрқ‘Ө\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(|v-w|)=\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v)\Delta\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(w), that are not already counted in ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap}.

Recall that we defined pв„“вүЎ(1вҲ’1/m)kвҖӢв„“subscriptрқ‘қв„“superscript11рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳв„“p\_{\ell}\equiv(1-1/m)^{k\ell} in Lemma [42](#Thmtheorem42 "Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").
Then,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | pnвүЎ1вҲ’1mвҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]=1вҲ’1mвҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–BвҖӢvвҖ–0],pnvвүЎ1вҲ’1mвҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–BвҖӢvвҖ–0],pnwвүЎ1вҲ’1mвҖӢрқ”јвҖӢ[вҖ–BвҖӢwвҖ–0]formulae-sequencesubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ11рқ‘ҡрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…11рқ‘ҡрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ј0formulae-sequencesubscriptрқ‘қsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ј11рқ‘ҡрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ј0subscriptрқ‘қsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө11рқ‘ҡрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptnormрқҗөрқ‘Ө0p\_{n}\equiv 1-\frac{1}{m}{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]=1-\frac{1}{m}{\mathbb{E}}[\|Bv\|\_{0}],\;\;\;\;p\_{n\_{v}}\equiv 1-\frac{1}{m}{\mathbb{E}}[\|Bv\|\_{0}],\;\;\;\;p\_{n\_{w}}\equiv 1-\frac{1}{m}{\mathbb{E}}[\|Bw\|\_{0}] |  |

Using LemmaВ [42](#Thmtheorem42 "Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") and ([8](#S7.E8 "In Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), and letting pvвҖӢwвүЎ(1вҲ’pnv)вҖӢ(1вҲ’pnw)subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө1subscriptрқ‘қsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ј1subscriptрқ‘қsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өp\_{vw}\equiv(1-p\_{n\_{v}})(1-p\_{n\_{w}}),

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]=mвҖӢ(1вҲ’pn)рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәО”]=mвҖӢpnвҖӢpvвҖӢw,andвҖӢpvвҖӢwвүӨkвҖӢnvmвҲ’1вӢ…kвҖӢnwmвҲ’1=k2вҖӢnvвҖӢnwm2вҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/m)).formulae-sequenceрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…рқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣрқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…О”рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Өandsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘ӨвӢ…рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ1superscriptрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘ҡ21рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘ҡ\begin{split}{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]&=m(1-p\_{n})\\ {\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\Delta}]&=mp\_{n}p\_{vw},\mathrm{\ and\ }p\_{vw}\leq\frac{kn\_{v}}{m-1}\cdot\frac{kn\_{w}}{m-1}=\frac{k^{2}n\_{v}n\_{w}}{m^{2}}(1+O(1/m)).\end{split} |  | (12) |

where the latter is due to the fact that the probability that given entries x~isubscript~рқ‘Ҙрқ‘–{\tilde{x}}\_{i} and y~isubscript~рқ‘Ұрқ‘–{\tilde{y}}\_{i} contribute to x~вӢ…y~вӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘Ұ{\tilde{x}}\cdot{\tilde{y}} is the probability that (a) the nрқ‘ӣn entries of vcsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җv^{c} yield BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvc=0subscriptрқҗө

рқ‘–superscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ0B\_{i\*}v^{c}=0, and (b) that both entries x~isubscript~рқ‘Ҙрқ‘–{\tilde{x}}\_{i} and y~isubscript~рқ‘Ұрқ‘–{\tilde{y}}\_{i} are nonzero.
Note that the three events in (a) and (b) are independent, since suppвҒЎ(vc)suppsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v^{c}), suppвҒЎ(vвҲ’vc)suppрқ‘Јsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(v-v^{c}), and suppвҒЎ(wвҲ’vc)suppрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ\operatorname{{\text{supp}}}(w-v^{c}) are disjoint.

Suppose, for some ОөвҲ©,ОөT>0

subscriptрқңҖsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү
0{\varepsilon}\_{\cap},{\varepsilon}\_{T}>0,

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ОәвҲ©вүҘрқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]вҲ’ОөвҲ©ОәвүӨрқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]+ОөT,subscriptрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…subscriptрқңҖрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү\begin{split}\kappa\_{\cap}&\geq{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]-{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}\\ \kappa&\leq{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]+{\varepsilon}\_{T},\end{split} |  | (13) |

which holds with small failure probability, as shown below.

First, using these assumptions on ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} and Оәрқң…\kappa, we establish a lower bound on hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…h\_{m,k}(\kappa).
Since ОәО”вүҘ0subscriptрқң…О”0\kappa\_{\Delta}\geq 0,

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | вҲ’km~вҖӢhm,kвҖӢ(Оә)рқ‘ҳ~рқ‘ҡsubscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…\displaystyle-\frac{k}{{\tilde{m}}}h\_{m,k}(\kappa) | =logвҒЎ(1вҲ’Оәm)=logвҒЎ(1вҲ’ОәвҲ©+ОәО”m)absent1рқң…рқ‘ҡ1subscriptрқң…subscriptрқң…О”рқ‘ҡ\displaystyle=\log(1-\frac{\kappa}{m})=\log(1-\frac{\kappa\_{\cap}+\kappa\_{\Delta}}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’ОәвҲ©m)absent1subscriptрқң…рқ‘ҡ\displaystyle\leq\log(1-\frac{\kappa\_{\cap}}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]вҲ’ОөвҲ©m)absent1рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҡ\displaystyle\leq\log(1-\frac{{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]-{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |

|  |  | =logвҒЎ(pn+ОөвҲ©m)absentsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҡ\displaystyle=\log(p\_{n}+\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{m}) |  |

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨвҲ’km~вҖӢ(nвҲ’ОөвҲ©kвҖӢpn),В usingВ вҖӢ(вҖӢ[11](#S7.E11 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ)вҖӢВ and the definition ofВ вҖӢpв„“вҖӢ, and soabsent  рқ‘ҳ~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣВ usingВ italic-([11](#S7.E11 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")italic-)В and the definition ofВ subscriptрқ‘қв„“, and so\displaystyle\leq-\frac{k}{{\tilde{m}}}(n-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{kp\_{n}}),\text{ using }\eqref{eq tm}\text{ and the definition of }p\_{\ell}\text{, and so} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…\displaystyle h\_{m,k}(\kappa) | вүҘnвҲ’ОөвҲ©kвҖӢpn.absentрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ\displaystyle\geq n-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{kp\_{n}}. |  |

If we assume that mвүҘ2вҖӢkвҖӢn+1рқ‘ҡ2рқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ1m\geq 2kn+1, then pnвүҘ1/2subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ12p\_{n}\geq 1/2.
We have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)вҲ’nвүҘвҲ’ОөвҲ©kвҖӢpnвүҘвҲ’2вҖӢОөвҲ©k,subscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…рқ‘ӣsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ2subscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҳh\_{m,k}(\kappa)-n\geq-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{kp\_{n}}\geq-\frac{2{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}}{k}, |  | (14) |

Again, using our assumptions on the sizes of ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} and Оәрқң…\kappa, we can obtain an upper bound on hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…h\_{m,k}(\kappa)

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…\displaystyle h\_{m,k}(\kappa) | =вҲ’m~kвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’Оәm)absent~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ1рқң…рқ‘ҡ\displaystyle=\frac{-{\tilde{m}}}{k}\log(1-\frac{\kappa}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨвҲ’m~kвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]+ОөTm)absent~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ1рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡ\displaystyle\leq\frac{-{\tilde{m}}}{k}\log(1-\frac{{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]+{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =вҲ’m~kвҖӢlogвҒЎ(pnвҲ’pnвҖӢpvвҖӢwвҲ’ОөTm)absent~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘ӨsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡ\displaystyle=\frac{-{\tilde{m}}}{k}\log(p\_{n}-p\_{n}p\_{vw}-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{m}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =nвҲ’m~kвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’pvвҖӢwвҲ’ОөTmвҖӢpn)absentрқ‘ӣ~рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘ӨsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ\displaystyle=n-\frac{{\tilde{m}}}{k}\log(1-p\_{vw}-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{mp\_{n}}) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨnвҲ’mkвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1вҲ’pvвҖӢwвҲ’ОөTmвҖӢpn)вҖӢВ usingВ вҖӢ(вҖӢ[11](#S7.E11 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ)absentрқ‘ӣрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘ӨsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣВ usingВ italic-([11](#S7.E11 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")italic-)\displaystyle\leq n-\frac{m}{k}\log(1-p\_{vw}-\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{mp\_{n}})\text{ using }\eqref{eq tm} |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨn+mkвҖӢpvвҖӢw+mkвҖӢОөTmвҖӢpnвҖӢ(1вҲ’pvвҖӢw),usingвҖӢ(вҖӢ[9](#S7.E9 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ)absent  рқ‘ӣрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Өusingitalic-([9](#S7.E9 "In 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")italic-)\displaystyle\leq n+\frac{m}{k}p\_{vw}+\frac{m}{k}\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{mp\_{n}(1-p\_{vw})},\mathrm{\ using\ }\eqref{eq log ineq} |  | (15) |

Assume that

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | mвүҘmaxвҒЎ{kвҖӢ2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw+1,2вҖӢkвҖӢn+1}.рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө12рқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ1m\geq\max\{k\sqrt{2n\_{v}n\_{w}}+1,2kn+1\}. |  | (16) |

which includes the prior assumption on mрқ‘ҡm.
Then using ([8](#S7.E8 "In Lemma 42. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and ([12](#S7.E12 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")),

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | 1вҲ’pvвҖӢwвүҘ1вҲ’kвҖӢnvmвҲ’1вӢ…kвҖӢnwmвҲ’1вүҘ1/21subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө1вӢ…рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ1121-p\_{vw}\geq 1-\frac{kn\_{v}}{m-1}\cdot\frac{kn\_{w}}{m-1}\geq 1/2 |  |

so pnвҖӢ(1вҲ’pvвҖӢw)вүҘ1/4subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө14p\_{n}(1-p\_{vw})\geq 1/4.
Therefore, from ([15](#S7.E15 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")),

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | kmвҖӢ(hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)вҲ’n)вүӨpvвҖӢw+ОөTmвҖӢpnвҖӢ(1вҲ’pvвҖӢw)вүӨpvвҖӢw+4вҖӢОөTm,рқ‘ҳрқ‘ҡsubscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…рқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘ӨsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘ӣ1subscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Өsubscriptрқ‘қрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө4subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҡ\frac{k}{m}(h\_{m,k}(\kappa)-n)\leq p\_{vw}+\frac{{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{mp\_{n}(1-p\_{vw})}\leq p\_{vw}+\frac{4{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{m}, |  |

and so

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)вҲ’nвүӨ[kвҖӢnvвҖӢnwm+4вҖӢОөTk]вҖӢ(1+OвҖӢ(1/m)),usingвҖӢ(вҖӢ[12](#S7.E12 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ).subscriptв„Һ  рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…рқ‘ӣ  delimited-[]рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ4subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҳ1рқ‘Ӯ1рқ‘ҡusingitalic-([12](#S7.E12 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")italic-)h\_{m,k}(\kappa)-n\leq\left[\frac{kn\_{v}n\_{w}}{m}+\frac{4{\varepsilon}\_{T}}{k}\right](1+O(1/m)),\mathrm{\ using}\eqref{eq kappas}. |  | (17) |

Both ([14](#S7.E14 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) and ([17](#S7.E17 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) control how close hm,kвҖӢ(Оә)subscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқң…h\_{m,k}(\kappa) is to nрқ‘ӣn, but they rely on the assumptions in ([13](#S7.E13 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).
We now need to bound PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ©вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]вүӨвҲ’ОөвҲ©]Prsubscriptрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…subscriptрқңҖ\Pr[\kappa\_{\cap}-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]\leq-{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}] and
PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]вүҘОөT]Prрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү\Pr[\kappa-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]\geq{\varepsilon}\_{T}], so that ([13](#S7.E13 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) holds with high probability.

Recall that ОәвҲ©=вҖ–BвҖӢvcвҖ–0subscriptрқң…subscriptnormрқҗөsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ0\kappa\_{\cap}=\|Bv^{c}\|\_{0}.
We can express ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} as ОәвҲ©вҖӢ(X1,X2,вҖҰ,XkвҖӢn)subscriptрқң…subscriptрқ‘Ӣ1subscriptрқ‘Ӣ2вҖҰsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ\kappa\_{\cap}(X\_{1},X\_{2},\ldots,X\_{kn}), where each Xв„“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“X\_{\ell} makes a random choice iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m] and sets BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvcsubscriptрқҗө

рқ‘–superscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җB\_{i\*}v^{c} to one; such choices are made kрқ‘ҳk times for each of the nрқ‘ӣn entries of vcsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җv^{c} that are equal to one.
To apply TheoremВ [28](#Thmtheorem28 "Theorem 28 ([ying_mcdiarmids_2004]). вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), bounds on BвҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)рқҗөsubscriptрқң…B(\kappa\_{\cap}) and the VariвҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)subscriptVarрқ‘–subscriptрқң…{\textbf{Var}}\_{i}(\kappa\_{\cap}) are needed.

Given choices for all other Xв„“вҖІsubscriptрқ‘Ӣsuperscriptв„“вҖІX\_{\ell^{\prime}}, a choice iрқ‘–i for Xв„“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“X\_{\ell} changes ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} if and only if given those other choices, BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvsubscriptрқҗө

рқ‘–рқ‘ЈB\_{i\*}v is equal to zero.
The only effect of these other choices is the number of bins already with ones, that is, the number of iвҖІsuperscriptрқ‘–вҖІi^{\prime} with BiвҖІвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢvc=1subscriptрқҗө

superscriptрқ‘–вҖІsuperscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘җ1B\_{i^{\prime}\*}v^{c}=1.
Given that rрқ‘ҹr bins have ones, the expected value of ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} with respect to the random choice Xв„“subscriptрқ‘Ӣв„“X\_{\ell} is 1вҲ’r/m1рқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡ1-r/m, and the most ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap} can differ from this is 1вҲ’r/mвүӨ11рқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡ11-r/m\leq 1, since it can hit one of those rрқ‘ҹr bins that are already one.
The variance Varв„“вҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)subscriptVarв„“subscriptрқң…{\textbf{Var}}\_{\ell}(\kappa\_{\cap}) is r/mвҲ’(r/m)2вүӨr/mвүӨ(kвҖӢnвҲ’1)/mрқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡsuperscriptрқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡ2рқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ1рқ‘ҡr/m-(r/m)^{2}\leq r/m\leq(kn-1)/m, the variance of a Bernoulli random variable with probability 1вҲ’r/m1рқ‘ҹрқ‘ҡ1-r/m of being one, and zero otherwise.
Thus Пғ~вҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)вүӨ(kвҖӢn)2/m~рқңҺsubscriptрқң…superscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡ{\tilde{\sigma}}(\kappa\_{\cap})\leq(kn)^{2}/m.333Put in a common setting, the bound of [broder\_network\_2004] corresponds to putting into the tail estimate denominator a value of kвҖӢnвүҘ(kвҖӢn)2/mрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣsuperscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡkn\geq(kn)^{2}/m for mвүҘkвҖӢnрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣm\geq kn, and the bound of [kamath\_tail\_1995] quoted in [bose\_false-positive\_2008] corresponds to mвүҘ(kвҖӢn)2/mрқ‘ҡsuperscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡm\geq(kn)^{2}/m for mвүҘkвҖӢnрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣm\geq kn.
From TheoremВ [28](#Thmtheorem28 "Theorem 28 ([ying_mcdiarmids_2004]). вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), if ОөвҲ©=kвҖӢОө/4subscriptрқңҖрқ‘ҳрқңҖ4{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}=k{\varepsilon}/4 for given Оө>0рқңҖ0{\varepsilon}>0, then

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ©вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәвҲ©]вүӨвҲ’ОөвҲ©]Prsubscriptрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…subscriptрқңҖ\displaystyle\Pr[\kappa\_{\cap}-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\cap}]\leq-{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢОөвҲ©2Пғ~вҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)+ОөвҲ©вҖӢBвҖӢ(ОәвҲ©)/3)вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢОөвҲ©2(kвҖӢn)2/m+ОөвҲ©/3)absent2superscriptsubscriptрқңҖ2~рқңҺsubscriptрқң…subscriptрқңҖрқҗөsubscriptрқң…32superscriptsubscriptрқңҖ2superscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқңҖ3\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}^{2}}{{\tilde{\sigma}}(\kappa\_{\cap})+{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}B(\kappa\_{\cap})/3}\right)\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}^{2}}{(kn)^{2}/m+{\varepsilon}\_{\cap}/3}\right) |  |

Leaving aside for the moment the values needed for mрқ‘ҡm and kрқ‘ҳk, we consider next
PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]вүҘОөT]Prрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү\Pr[\kappa-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]\geq{\varepsilon}\_{T}].
Here from Оә=ОәвҲ©+ОәО”рқң…subscriptрқң…subscriptрқң…О”\kappa=\kappa\_{\cap}+\kappa\_{\Delta}, we can regard Оәрқң…\kappa as the function of 2вҖӢkвҖӢn+2вҖӢkвҖӢnv+2вҖӢkвҖӢnw2рқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ј2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө2kn+2kn\_{v}+2kn\_{w} random variables, of which the first 2вҖӢkвҖӢn2рқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2kn, from ОәвҲ©subscriptрқң…\kappa\_{\cap}, have Пғ~~рқңҺ{\tilde{\sigma}} contribution at most (kвҖӢn)2/msuperscriptрқ‘ҳрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡ(kn)^{2}/m and BвүӨ1рқҗө1B\leq 1.
The next 2вҖӢkвҖӢnv2рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ј2kn\_{v}, representing the choices made that result in x~~рқ‘Ҙ{\tilde{x}}, each have the property that their mean and variance, as a function of the choices of all the other variables, depend only on the number of ones in y~~рқ‘Ұ{\tilde{y}}: the minimum mean is 1вҲ’kвҖӢnw1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө1-kn\_{w}, so the contribution to BрқҗөB is at most 1вҲ’kвҖӢnwвүӨ11рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө11-kn\_{w}\leq 1; the maximum variance is
(kвҖӢnw/m)вҖӢ(1вҲ’(kвҖӢnw/m))вүӨkвҖӢnw/mрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ1рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ(kn\_{w}/m)(1-(kn\_{w}/m))\leq kn\_{w}/m.
There are kвҖӢnvрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јkn\_{v} such variables, so the contribution to Пғ~~рқңҺ{\tilde{\sigma}} is (kвҖӢnv)вҖӢ(kвҖӢnw/m)рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ(kn\_{v})(kn\_{w}/m).
Similarly, the last kвҖӢnwрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өkn\_{w} random choices have BвүӨ1рқҗө1B\leq 1 and contribution to Пғ~~рқңҺ{\tilde{\sigma}} of (kвҖӢnw)вҖӢ(kвҖӢnv/m)рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘ҡ(kn\_{w})(kn\_{v}/m).
So BвҖӢ(Оә)вүӨ1рқҗөрқң…1B(\kappa)\leq 1, and Пғ~вҖӢ(Оә)вүӨk2вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m~рқңҺрқң…superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ{\tilde{\sigma}}(\kappa)\leq k^{2}(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m.
If ОөT=kвҖӢОө/4subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқ‘ҳрқңҖ4{\varepsilon}\_{T}=k{\varepsilon}/4, we have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]вүҘОөT]Prрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү\displaystyle\Pr[\kappa-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]\geq{\varepsilon}\_{T}] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢОөT2Пғ~вҖӢ(Оә)+ОөTвҖӢBвҖӢ(Оә)/3)вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢОөT2k2вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m+ОөT/3)absent2superscriptsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү2~рқңҺрқң…subscriptрқңҖрқ‘Үрқҗөрқң…32superscriptsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү2superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡsubscriptрқңҖрқ‘Ү3\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2{\varepsilon}\_{T}^{2}}{{\tilde{\sigma}}(\kappa)+{\varepsilon}\_{T}B(\kappa)/3}\right)\leq\exp\left(-\frac{2{\varepsilon}\_{T}^{2}}{k^{2}(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m+{\varepsilon}\_{T}/3}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =expвҒЎ(вҲ’2вҖӢ(kвҖӢОө/4)2k2вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m+(kвҖӢОө/4)/3)absent2superscriptрқ‘ҳрқңҖ42superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқңҖ43\displaystyle=\exp\left(-\frac{2(k{\varepsilon}/4)^{2}}{k^{2}(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m+(k{\varepsilon}/4)/3}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =expвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө28вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m+2вҖӢОө/3вҖӢk).absentsuperscriptрқңҖ28superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ2рқңҖ3рқ‘ҳ\displaystyle=\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{8(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m+2{\varepsilon}/3k}\right). |  | (19) |

If ([7.1](#S7.Ex148 "Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) yields a bound of Оҙ/2рқӣҝ2\delta/2, ([7.1](#S7.Ex147 "Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) will too, and the total failure probability will be at most Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.

Assume WLOG that nwвүҘnvsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јn\_{w}\geq n\_{v}.
From ([17](#S7.E17 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), for the mean of Оәрқң…\kappa to be at most ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon}, we must have mвүҘkвҖӢnvвҖӢnw/2вҖӢОөрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө2рқңҖm\geq kn\_{v}n\_{w}/2{\varepsilon}.
This implies that in ([7.1](#S7.Ex148 "Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), 8вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m+2вҖӢОө/3вҖӢkвүӨ8вҖӢn2/m+c1вҖӢОө/k8superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ2рқңҖ3рқ‘ҳ8superscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘җ1рқңҖрқ‘ҳ8(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m+2{\varepsilon}/3k\leq 8n^{2}/m+c\_{1}{\varepsilon}/k, for c1=32+23subscriptрқ‘җ13223c\_{1}=32+\frac{2}{3}.
For 8вҖӢn2/m8superscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡ8n^{2}/m to not dominate c1вҖӢОө/ksubscriptрқ‘җ1рқңҖрқ‘ҳc\_{1}{\varepsilon}/k in the sum 8вҖӢn2/m+c1вҖӢОө/k8superscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘җ1рқңҖрқ‘ҳ8n^{2}/m+c\_{1}{\varepsilon}/k, we need mвүҘ8вҖӢkвҖӢc1вҖӢn2/Оөрқ‘ҡ8рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘җ1superscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқңҖm\geq 8kc\_{1}n^{2}/{\varepsilon}, yielding
2вҖӢc1вҖӢОө/k2subscriptрқ‘җ1рқңҖрқ‘ҳ2c\_{1}{\varepsilon}/k in the denominator, so that under these assumptions regardingВ mрқ‘ҡm,

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[ОәО”вҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[ОәО”]вүҘОө]Prsubscriptрқң…О”рқ”јdelimited-[]subscriptрқң…О”рқңҖ\displaystyle\Pr[\kappa\_{\Delta}-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa\_{\Delta}]\geq{\varepsilon}] | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө28вҖӢ(n2+2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw)/m+2вҖӢОө/3вҖӢk)absentsuperscriptрқңҖ28superscriptрқ‘ӣ22subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ2рқңҖ3рқ‘ҳ\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{8(n^{2}+2n\_{v}n\_{w})/m+2{\varepsilon}/3k}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө22вҖӢc1вҖӢОө/k)=expвҒЎ(вҲ’kвҖӢОө/2вҖӢc1)вүӨОҙ/2вҖӢforвҖӢk=2вҖӢc1вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)/Оө.absentsuperscriptрқңҖ22subscriptрқ‘җ1рқңҖрқ‘ҳрқ‘ҳрқңҖ2subscriptрқ‘җ1рқӣҝ2forрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘җ12рқӣҝрқңҖ\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{2c\_{1}{\varepsilon}/k}\right)=\exp(-k{\varepsilon}/2c\_{1})\leq\delta/2\mathrm{\ for\ }k=2c\_{1}\log(2/\delta)/{\varepsilon}. |  |

With a similar bound for PrвҒЎ[ОәвҲ’рқ”јвҖӢ[Оә]вүӨвҲ’Оө]Prрқң…рқ”јdelimited-[]рқң…рқңҖ\Pr[\kappa-{\mathbb{E}}[\kappa]\leq-{\varepsilon}], via ([14](#S7.E14 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.1 Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")),
we have that mвүҘkОөвҖӢ(nvвҖӢnw/2+8вҖӢc1вҖӢn2+ОөвҖӢ(n+nw))рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқңҖsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө28subscriptрқ‘җ1superscriptрқ‘ӣ2рқңҖрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өm\geq\frac{k}{{\varepsilon}}(n\_{v}n\_{w}/2+8c\_{1}n^{2}+{\varepsilon}(n+n\_{w})) with k=2вҖӢc1вҖӢlogвҒЎ(2/Оҙ)/Оөрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘җ12рқӣҝрқңҖk=2c\_{1}\log(2/\delta)/{\varepsilon} suffices to obtain hm,kвҖӢ(xвӢ…y)=nВұОөsubscriptв„Һ

рқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұplus-or-minusрқ‘ӣрқңҖh\_{m,k}(x\cdot y)=n\pm{\varepsilon} with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.
The result follows.
вҲҺ

#### 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters

In another sparse binary model, bundling is done by addition in instead of disjunction, so a bundle is simply BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv instead of 1вҲ§BвҖӢv1рқҗөрқ‘Ј1\wedge Bv.
In the data structures literature, this is a *counting* variant of a Bloom filter.
Here BрқҗөB is chosen to be sparse in a slightly different way than for Bloom filters:
each atomic vector BвҲ—jsubscriptрқҗөabsentрқ‘—B\_{\*j} for jвҲҲ[m]рқ‘—delimited-[]рқ‘ҡj\in[m] has all vectors with kрқ‘ҳk ones equally likely, or equivalently, is created by starting from a vector of all zeros, in each trial picking iвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡi\in[m] uniformly at random, setting BiвҖӢjвҶ’1вҶ’subscriptрқҗөрқ‘–рқ‘—1B\_{ij}\rightarrow 1, until there are kрқ‘ҳk nonzeros.

When the sparsity is block-structured, that is, an atomic mрқ‘ҡm-vector has mрқ‘ҡm divisible byВ kрқ‘ҳk, and there areВ kрқ‘ҳk blocks each with exactly one nonzero entry, then the resulting bundling is called a *count-min sketch* in the data structures literature, and the Sparse Block Codes model in the VSA literature.
See [cormode\_improved\_2005] and [laiho\_high-dimensional\_2015] respectively for more information.

[cormode\_improved\_2005] showed that dot product estimation for two bundles can be done as a nonlinear operation: taking dot products of corresponding blocks and then the minimum of these kрқ‘ҳk dot products.
The resulting estimate Xрқ‘ӢX of vвӢ…wвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘Өv\cdot w using BвҖӢvрқҗөрқ‘ЈBv and BвҖӢwрқҗөрқ‘ӨBw has vвӢ…wвүӨXвүӨvвӢ…w+ОөвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘Өрқ‘ӢвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘ӨрқңҖv\cdot w\leq X\leq v\cdot w+{\varepsilon} with failure probability Оҙрқӣҝ\delta, for m=kвҖӢmвҖІрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқ‘ҡвҖІm=km^{\prime} where k=OвҖӢ(logвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҳрқ‘Ӯ1рқӣҝk=O(\log(1/\delta)) and
mвҖІ=OвҖӢ(вҖ–vвҖ–1вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–1/Оө)superscriptрқ‘ҡвҖІрқ‘Ӯsubscriptnormрқ‘Ј1subscriptnormрқ‘Ө1рқңҖm^{\prime}=O(\|v\|\_{1}\|w\|\_{1}/{\varepsilon}).
For v,wвҲҲ{0,1}d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscript01рқ‘‘v,w\in\{0,1\}^{d}, the dimension mрқ‘ҡm needed for estimating set intersection size has a smaller dependence on ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon}, but possibly worse dependence on вҖ–vвҖ–1subscriptnormрқ‘Ј1\|v\|\_{1}, вҖ–wвҖ–1subscriptnormрқ‘Ө1\|w\|\_{1}, and vвӢ…wвӢ…рқ‘Јрқ‘Өv\cdot w
than what we showed for Bloom filters.
This is because вҖ–vвҖ–1вҖӢвҖ–wвҖ–1=(nv+n)вҖӢ(nw+n)вүҘnvвҖӢnw+n2subscriptnormрқ‘Ј1subscriptnormрқ‘Ө1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ӣsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsuperscriptрқ‘ӣ2\|v\|\_{1}\|w\|\_{1}=(n\_{v}+n)(n\_{w}+n)\geq n\_{v}n\_{w}+n^{2}, where nрқ‘ӣn, nvsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јn\_{v}, and nwsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өn\_{w} are defined in Theorem [22](#Thmtheorem22 "Theorem 22. вҖЈ 2.5 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures").

Beyond the setting above, vрқ‘Јv and wрқ‘Өw may have entries that are nonnegative integers, corresponding to multi-sets (sets where each element appears with some multiplicity).
Dot products for such multi-sets have applications in database operations.
However, one could also consider an analog of set intersection for multi-sets where the multiplicity of an element in the intersection is the minimum of its multiplicities in the two intersected multi-sets.
The size of the intersection, defined in this way, can also be estimated using bundles of sparse binary atomic vectors.
This operation will be analyzed next.
For x,yвҲҲIвҖӢRm

рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ
superscriptIRрқ‘ҡx,y\in\operatorname{{\mathrm{I\!R}}}^{m}, let xвҲ§yрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұx\wedge y denote the vector zрқ‘§z with zi=minвҒЎ{xi,yi}subscriptрқ‘§рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘–z\_{i}=\min\{x\_{i},y\_{i}\}.
As discussed, on nonnegative vectors, we define the operation
xвҲ§вӢ…yвүЎвҖ–xвҲ§yвҖ–1=вҲ‘iвҲҲ[m]minвҒЎ{xi,yi}fragmentsfragmentsвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұsubscriptnormрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ1subscriptрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ұрқ‘–x\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}y\equiv\|x\wedge y\|\_{1}=\sum\_{i\in[m]}\min\{x\_{i},y\_{i}\}.
Note that вҖ–xвҲ’yвҖ–1=вҖ–xвҖ–1+вҖ–yвҖ–1вҲ’2вҖӢ(xвҲ§вӢ…y)subscriptnormрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ1subscriptnormрқ‘Ҙ1subscriptnormрқ‘Ұ12fragmentsfragmentsвӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ\|x-y\|\_{1}=\|x\|\_{1}+\|y\|\_{1}-2(x\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}y), analogous to
вҖ–xвҲ’yвҖ–22=вҖ–xвҖ–22+вҖ–yвҖ–22вҲ’2вҖӢ(xвӢ…y)superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ22superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘Ҙ22superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘Ұ222вӢ…рқ‘Ҙрқ‘Ұ\|x-y\|\_{2}^{2}=\|x\|\_{2}^{2}+\|y\|\_{2}^{2}-2(x\cdot y).

##### Theorem (Restatement of Theorem [23](#Thmtheorem23 "Theorem 23. вҖЈ 2.5 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis вҖЈ 2 Technical Overview and Statements of Results вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")).

Let v,wвҲҲв„қвүҘ0d

рқ‘Јрқ‘Ө
superscriptsubscriptв„қabsent0рқ‘‘v,w\in{\mathbb{R}}\_{\geq 0}^{d}. Let KbвүЎвҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–вҲһвүӨmaxвҒЎ{вҖ–vвҖ–вҲһ,вҖ–wвҖ–вҲһ}subscriptрқҗҫрқ‘Ҹsubscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Өsubscriptnormрқ‘Јsubscriptnormрқ‘ӨK\_{b}\equiv\|v-w\|\_{\infty}\leq\max\{\|v\|\_{\infty},\|w\|\_{\infty}\}, and define:

|  |  |  |

Let x=BвҖӢvрқ‘Ҙрқҗөрқ‘Јx=Bv and y=BвҖӢwрқ‘Ұрқҗөрқ‘Өy=Bw, where BвҲҲ{0,1}mГ—dрқҗөsuperscript01рқ‘ҡрқ‘‘B\in\{0,1\}^{m\times d} is a sparse binary matrix.
Then, for ОҙвҲҲ(0,1)рқӣҝ01\delta\in(0,1) and Оө>0рқңҖ0{\varepsilon}>0, there are
k=OвҖӢ(KbвҖӢОөвҲ’1вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҳрқ‘Ӯsubscriptрқҗҫрқ‘ҸsuperscriptрқңҖ11рқӣҝk=O(K\_{b}{\varepsilon}^{-1}\log(1/\delta)) and m=12вҖӢПҖ2вҖӢkвҖӢОөвҲ’1вҖӢnvвҖӢnw=OвҖӢ(KbвҖӢОөвҲ’2вҖӢnvвҖӢnwвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡ12superscriptрқңӢ2рқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқңҖ1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘Ӯsubscriptрқҗҫрқ‘ҸsuperscriptрқңҖ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө1рқӣҝm=12\pi^{2}k{\varepsilon}^{-1}n\_{v}n\_{w}=O(K\_{b}{\varepsilon}^{-2}n\_{v}n\_{w}\log(1/\delta)) such that

with failure probability at mostВ Оҙрқӣҝ\delta.
Since nv+nw=вҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө1n\_{v}+n\_{w}=\|v-w\|\_{1}, m=OвҖӢ(KbвҖӢОөвҲ’2вҖӢвҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–12вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))рқ‘ҡрқ‘Ӯsubscriptрқҗҫрқ‘ҸsuperscriptрқңҖ2superscriptsubscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө121рқӣҝm=O(K\_{b}{\varepsilon}^{-2}\|v-w\|\_{1}^{2}\log(1/\delta)) also suffices (using the AM-GM inequality on nvвҖӢnwsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өn\_{v}n\_{w}).
If вҖ–vвҖ–1,вҖ–wвҖ–1

subscriptnormрқ‘Ј1subscriptnormрқ‘Ө1\|v\|\_{1},\|w\|\_{1} are stored, then вҖ–vвҲ’wвҖ–1subscriptnormрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө1\|v-w\|\_{1} can be estimated up to additive ОөрқңҖ{\varepsilon} with the sameВ mрқ‘ҡm.

##### Proof.

Let v~вүЎvвҲ’(vвҲ§w)~рқ‘Јрқ‘Јрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө{\tilde{v}}\equiv v-(v\wedge w), w~вүЎwвҲ’(vвҲ§w)~рқ‘Өрқ‘Өрқ‘Јрқ‘Ө{\tilde{w}}\equiv w-(v\wedge w) and x~вүЎBвҖӢv~~рқ‘Ҙрқҗө~рқ‘Ј{\tilde{x}}\equiv B{\tilde{v}}, y~вүЎBвҖӢw~~рқ‘Ұрқҗө~рқ‘Ө{\tilde{y}}\equiv B{\tilde{w}}.
Note that nv=вҖ–v~вҖ–1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptnorm~рқ‘Ј1n\_{v}=\|{\tilde{v}}\|\_{1}, nw=вҖ–w~вҖ–1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өsubscriptnorm~рқ‘Ө1n\_{w}=\|{\tilde{w}}\|\_{1}.
Using minвҒЎ{c+a,c+b}=c+minвҒЎ{a,b}рқ‘җрқ‘Һрқ‘җрқ‘Ҹрқ‘җрқ‘Һрқ‘Ҹ\min\{c+a,c+b\}=c+\min\{a,b\}, we have

рқ‘–~рқ‘ЈB\_{i\*}{\tilde{v}} is independent of BiвҒЈвҲ—вҖӢw~subscriptрқҗө

рқ‘–~рқ‘ӨB\_{i\*}{\tilde{w}}.
Therefore,

|  | PrвҒЎ[x~iвҲ§y~iвүҘz]=PrвҒЎ[x~iвүҘz]вҖӢPrвҒЎ[y~iвүҘz]Prsubscript~рқ‘Ҙрқ‘–subscript~рқ‘Ұрқ‘–рқ‘§Prsubscript~рқ‘Ҙрқ‘–рқ‘§Prsubscript~рқ‘Ұрқ‘–рқ‘§\Pr[{\tilde{x}}\_{i}\wedge{\tilde{y}}\_{i}\geq z]=\Pr[{\tilde{x}}\_{i}\geq z]\Pr[{\tilde{y}}\_{i}\geq z] |  |

Thus

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[x~вҲ§вӢ…y~]вүӨПҖ26вӢ…k2вҖӢnvвҖӢnwm.рқ”јdelimited-[]fragmentsfragmentsвӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқңӢ26superscriptрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡ{\mathbb{E}}[{\tilde{x}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}{\tilde{y}}]\leq\frac{\pi^{2}}{6}\cdot\frac{k^{2}n\_{v}n\_{w}}{m}. |  | (36) |

It remains to show that x~вҲ§вӢ…y~fragmentsfragmentsвӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘Ұ{\tilde{x}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}{\tilde{y}} concentrates.
We will use the Bernstein form of McDiarmidвҖҷs inequality (TheoremВ [28](#Thmtheorem28 "Theorem 28 ([ying_mcdiarmids_2004]). вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")), showing concentration of a function fвҖӢ(X)рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣf(X).
Here XвҲҲ[m]ntрқ‘Ӣsuperscriptdelimited-[]рқ‘ҡsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘ЎX\in[m]^{n\_{t}} for ntвүЎkвҖӢвҖ–v~+w~вҖ–0вүӨkвҖӢ(nv+nw)subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ўрқ‘ҳsubscriptnorm~рқ‘Ј~рқ‘Ө0рқ‘ҳsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өn\_{t}\equiv k\|{\tilde{v}}+{\tilde{w}}\|\_{0}\leq k(n\_{v}+n\_{w}), and each Xrsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҹX\_{r}, for rвҲҲ[nt]рқ‘ҹdelimited-[]subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ўr\in[n\_{t}], maps to a column jрқ‘—j of BрқҗөB where v~j+w~j>0subscript~рқ‘Јрқ‘—subscript~рқ‘Өрқ‘—0{\tilde{v}}\_{j}+{\tilde{w}}\_{j}>0, and for random i=XrвҲҲ[m]рқ‘–subscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҹdelimited-[]рқ‘ҡi=X\_{r}\in[m], BiвҖӢjsubscriptрқҗөрқ‘–рқ‘—B\_{ij} is incremented by one.
The function fвҖӢ(X)рқ‘“рқ‘Ӣf(X) is then fвҖӢ(X)=BвҖӢv~вҲ§вӢ…BвҖӢw~рқ‘“рқ‘ӢfragmentsfragmentsвӢ…рқҗө~рқ‘Јрқҗө~рқ‘Өf(X)=B{\tilde{v}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}B{\tilde{w}}, where BрқҗөB is determined by Xрқ‘ӢX.
To use TheoremВ [28](#Thmtheorem28 "Theorem 28 ([ying_mcdiarmids_2004]). вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"), we need to bound Пғ~вҖӢ(f)~рқңҺрқ‘“{\tilde{\sigma}}(f) and BвҖӢ(f)рқҗөрқ‘“B(f) of that theorem, bounding the effects of changes of single entries of Xрқ‘ӢX.

Suppose BвҖІsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІB^{\prime} is the result of the choices of Xрқ‘ӢX, for all entries except for entry Xrsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҹX\_{r}, where Xrsubscriptрқ‘Ӣрқ‘ҹX\_{r} maps to column jрқ‘—j, and to a random IвҲҲ[m]рқҗјdelimited-[]рқ‘ҡI\in[m].
Then the resulting B=BвҖІ+eIвҖӢejвҠӨрқҗөsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІsubscriptрқ‘’рқҗјsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—topB=B^{\prime}+e\_{I}e\_{j}^{\top}, where ejвҲҲ{0,1}dsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—superscript01рқ‘‘e\_{j}\in\{0,1\}^{d} (with the 111 in the jрқ‘—j position) and eIвҲҲ{0,1}msubscriptрқ‘’рқҗјsuperscript01рқ‘ҡe\_{I}\in\{0,1\}^{m} (with the 111 in the IрқҗјI position) are natural basis vectors, and
BвҖӢv=BвҖІвҖӢv+eIвҖӢejвҠӨвҖӢv=BвҖІвҖӢv+vjвҖӢeIрқҗөрқ‘ЈsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘’рқҗјsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—topрқ‘ЈsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘Јрқ‘—subscriptрқ‘’рқҗјBv=B^{\prime}v+e\_{I}e\_{j}^{\top}v=B^{\prime}v+v\_{j}e\_{I}.

Here giвҖӢ(X,y)subscriptрқ‘”рқ‘–рқ‘Ӣрқ‘Ұg\_{i}(X,y) of TheoremВ [28](#Thmtheorem28 "Theorem 28 ([ying_mcdiarmids_2004]). вҖЈ 3 Preliminaries and Concentration Inequalities вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures") corresponds to
gвҖӢ(BвҖІ,j,I)=(BвҖІ+eIвҖӢejвҠӨ)вҖӢv~вҲ§вӢ…(BвҖІ+eIвҖӢejвҠӨ)вҖӢw~рқ‘”superscriptрқҗөвҖІрқ‘—рқҗјfragmentsfragmentsвӢ…superscriptрқҗөвҖІsubscriptрқ‘’рқҗјsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—top~рқ‘ЈsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІsubscriptрқ‘’рқҗјsuperscriptsubscriptрқ‘’рқ‘—top~рқ‘Өg(B^{\prime},j,I)=(B^{\prime}+e\_{I}e\_{j}^{\top}){\tilde{v}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}(B^{\prime}+e\_{I}e\_{j}^{\top}){\tilde{w}},
and we need to bound, over all BвҖІsuperscriptрқҗөвҖІB^{\prime} and jрқ‘—j, VariвҖӢ[gвҖӢ(BвҖІ,j,i)]subscriptVarрқ‘–delimited-[]рқ‘”superscriptрқҗөвҖІрқ‘—рқ‘–{\textbf{Var}}\_{i}[g(B^{\prime},j,i)] and
maxi|g(BвҖІ,j,i)вҲ’рқ”јiвҖІg(BвҖІ,j,iвҖІ)]|\max\_{i}|g(B^{\prime},j,i)-{\mathbb{E}}\_{i^{\prime}}g(B^{\prime},j,i^{\prime})]|.
Again noting that because addition distributes over minimization, we can let

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’k2вҖӢОө2/2(2вҖӢk2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw/m)+kвҖӢОөвҖӢKb/6)fromвҖӢ(вҖӢ[47](#S7.E47 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ),(вҖӢ[46](#S7.E46 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")вҖӢ)absent  superscriptрқ‘ҳ2superscriptрқңҖ222superscriptрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡрқ‘ҳрқңҖsubscriptрқҗҫрқ‘Ҹ6from([47](#S7.E47 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"))([46](#S7.E46 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures"))\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{k^{2}{\varepsilon}^{2}/2}{(2k^{2}n\_{v}n\_{w}/m)+k{\varepsilon}K\_{b}/6}\right)\qquad\mathrm{\ from\ \eqref{eq tsig count},\eqref{eq B count}} |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | =expвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө24вҖӢnvвҖӢnw/m+kвҲ’1вҖӢОөвҖӢKb/3)=expвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө2nvвҖӢnw/(3вҖӢПҖ2вҖӢОөвҲ’2вҖӢnvвҖӢnwвҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))+Оө2/2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))absentsuperscriptрқңҖ24subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡsuperscriptрқ‘ҳ1рқңҖsubscriptрқҗҫрқ‘Ҹ3superscriptрқңҖ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө3superscriptрқңӢ2superscriptрқңҖ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө1рқӣҝsuperscriptрқңҖ221рқӣҝ\displaystyle=\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{4n\_{v}n\_{w}/m+k^{-1}{\varepsilon}K\_{b}/3}\right)=\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{n\_{v}n\_{w}/(3\pi^{2}{\varepsilon}^{-2}n\_{v}n\_{w}\log(1/\delta))+{\varepsilon}^{2}/2\log(1/\delta)}\right) |  |
|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | вүӨexpвҒЎ(вҲ’Оө2Оө2/2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ)+Оө2/2вҖӢlogвҒЎ(1/Оҙ))=Оҙ.absentsuperscriptрқңҖ2superscriptрқңҖ221рқӣҝsuperscriptрқңҖ221рқӣҝрқӣҝ\displaystyle\leq\exp\left(-\frac{{\varepsilon}^{2}}{{\varepsilon}^{2}/2\log(1/\delta)+{\varepsilon}^{2}/2\log(1/\delta)}\right)=\delta. |  |

We also need ([36](#S7.E36 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) to bound

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | рқ”јвҖӢ[x~вҲ§вӢ…y~]вүӨПҖ26вӢ…k2вҖӢnvвҖӢnwm=ПҖ26вӢ…k2вҖӢnvвҖӢnw12вҖӢПҖ2вҖӢkвҖӢОөвҲ’1вҖӢnvвҖӢnw=kвҖӢОө/2.рқ”јdelimited-[]fragmentsfragmentsвӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘ҰвӢ…superscriptрқңӢ26superscriptрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҡвӢ…superscriptрқңӢ26superscriptрқ‘ҳ2subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Ө12superscriptрқңӢ2рқ‘ҳsuperscriptрқңҖ1subscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Јsubscriptрқ‘ӣрқ‘Өрқ‘ҳрқңҖ2{\mathbb{E}}[{\tilde{x}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}{\tilde{y}}]\leq\frac{\pi^{2}}{6}\cdot\frac{k^{2}n\_{v}n\_{w}}{m}=\frac{\pi^{2}}{6}\cdot\frac{k^{2}n\_{v}n\_{w}}{12\pi^{2}k{\varepsilon}^{-1}n\_{v}n\_{w}}=k{\varepsilon}/2. |  |

Putting these together,

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | PrвҒЎ[x~вҲ§вӢ…y~вүҘkвҖӢОө]вүӨОҙ,PrfragmentsfragmentsвӢ…~рқ‘Ҙ~рқ‘Ұрқ‘ҳрқңҖрқӣҝ\Pr[{\tilde{x}}\mathbin{\ooalign{\hfil$\wedge$\hfil\cr\hfil$\cdot$\hfil\crcr}}{\tilde{y}}\geq k{\varepsilon}]\leq\delta, |  |

which with ([35](#S7.E35 "In Proof. вҖЈ 7.2 Counting Bloom Filters вҖЈ 7 Sparse Binary Bundling and Bloom Filter Analysis via Concentration вҖЈ Capacity Analysis of Vector Symbolic Architectures")) implies the result.
вҲҺ
